  - Filter by coordinates or handles.  
  - Jump directly to highlighted object.  
- **Benefit:** Saves 10+ minutes per search task → accuracy and speed.

- **Function:** Simplifies managing process control block data.  
- **Effective Utilization:**  
  - Standardized input for instrumentation/P&ID workflows.  
  - Links attributes to system properties.  
- **Benefit:** Reduces errors in P&ID drafting, consistent data entry.

- **Function:** Locate and edit objects by property/attribute.  
- **Effective Utilization:**  
  - Quickly navigate to blocks in large drawings.  
  - Edit multiple instances in one pass.  
- **Benefit:** Eliminates manual hunting, ensures nothing is missed.

- **Function:** Manage block tags (parent/child relationships).  
- **Effective Utilization:**

  - Automatically syncs attributes across related blocks.  
- **Benefit:** Maintains engineering data integrity.

- **Function:** View **XData, XRecords, and NOD data** in a grid.

- **Benefit:** Enforces CAD standards, prevents layer clutter.

- **Effective Utilization:**  
  - Review change logs.

  - UI with checkboxes for selective rollback.  
- **Benefit:** Provides safety net for bulk editing.

## Response:
10/1/2025, 3:18:56 PM

> **Considering AutoCAD UI options**
>
> To create a UI dropdown with image previews of AutoCAD block symbols, I’m thinking of using OwnerDraw ComboBox with image items or modifying ItemHeight and DrawMode. I recall the BlockTableRecord.PreviewIcon (a Bitmap), or possibly using preview icons like ThumbnailBitmap for rendering. Alternatively, pre-rendering small assets might be a quicker solution.
>
> **Proposing data loading strategy**
>
> For the code, I’ll load block definitions and try to get the PreviewIcon. If it’s null, I can sample the bounding box and render a simple preview. Alternatively, I could use AcDbRasterImage. I’m thinking about a custom ComboBox control, using C# 7.3 to follow compatibility. I’ll also use a BlockItem model for the items.
>
> Thought for 21s

Absolutely—this is doable and it looks slick. The gist is:

- Use a WinForms **ComboBox** on your palette with **OwnerDraw** to render each item as “icon + block name.”
- Populate it from the current drawing’s **BlockTable**.
- For each block, try to grab a **preview bitmap** (fastest path: `BlockTableRecord.PreviewIcon` if available; otherwise fall back to a cached placeholder).
- Cache the previews so you’re not hitting the DB every time the dropdown opens.

Here’s a clean, drop-in approach (C# 7.3 compatible).

# 1) A small model to hold items
```csharp
// v1.0.0 (2025-10-01)
// Purpose: Represents a block option with a preview icon for owner-drawn combo boxes.

using System.Drawing;

namespace AutoCAD.Forms
{
    public sealed class BlockItem
    {
        public string Name { get; }
        public Bitmap Icon { get; }   // 24–48 px tall works well

        public BlockItem(string name, Bitmap icon)
        {
            Name = name;
            Icon = icon;
        }

        public override string ToString() => Name; // safe fallback
    }
}
```

# 2) Service to collect blocks + previews (with caching)
```csharp
// v1.0.0 (2025-10-01)
// Purpose: Collect block names and preview icons from the current drawing.
// Notes: Skips anonymous/layout blocks; caches preview bitmaps.

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Drawing;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using AcApp = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application;

namespace AutoCAD.Forms
{
    public static class BlockPreviewService
    {
        // Simple in-proc cache so we don’t re-fetch previews constantly
        private static readonly Dictionary<string, Bitmap> _iconCache
            = new Dictionary<string, Bitmap>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        public static List<BlockItem> GetBlockItems(Bitmap fallbackIcon = null)
        {
            var items = new List<BlockItem>();

            var doc = AcApp.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return items;

            var db = doc.Database;

            using (doc.LockDocument())
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var bt = (BlockTable)tr.GetObject(db.BlockTableId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                foreach (ObjectId btrId in bt)
                {
                    var btr = tr.GetObject(btrId, OpenMode.ForRead) as BlockTableRecord;
                    if (btr == null) continue;

                    // Filter: skip anonymous, layouts, and xrefs
                    if (btr.IsLayout || btr.IsAnonymous || btr.IsFromExternalReference)
                        continue;

                    var name = btr.Name;

                    Bitmap icon;
                    if (!_iconCache.TryGetValue(name, out icon))
                    {
                        icon = TryGetPreview(btr) ?? fallbackIcon;
                        // Keep a small-ish cached copy
                        if (icon != null)
                            _iconCache[name] = ResizeToFit(icon, 32, 32);
                    }

                    items.Add(new BlockItem(name, _iconCache.ContainsKey(name) ? _iconCache[name] : icon));
                }

                tr.Commit();
            }

            // Sort by name for UX
            items.Sort((a, b) => string.Compare(a.Name, b.Name, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
            return items;
        }

        // Attempts to get a preview bitmap from the block table record
        private static Bitmap TryGetPreview(BlockTableRecord btr)
        {
            try
            {
                // Many AutoCAD versions expose PreviewIcon on BTR via .NET
                // If null, no preview was stored/available.
                return btr.PreviewIcon;
            }
            catch
            {
                // Some versions/blocks may throw; swallow and fallback.
                return null;
            }
        }

        // Utility: keep aspect ratio, fit within w x h
        private static Bitmap ResizeToFit(Bitmap src, int maxW, int maxH)
        {
            if (src == null) return null;

            float scale = Math.Min(maxW / (float)src.Width, maxH / (float)src.Height);
            if (scale >= 1f) return new Bitmap(src); // already small

            int w = Math.Max(1, (int)Math.Round(src.Width * scale));
            int h = Math.Max(1, (int)Math.Round(src.Height * scale));

            var bmp = new Bitmap(w, h);
            using (var g = Graphics.FromImage(bmp))
            {
                g.InterpolationMode = System.Drawing.Drawing2D.InterpolationMode.HighQualityBicubic;
                g.Clear(Color.Transparent);
                g.DrawImage(src, 0, 0, w, h);
            }
            return bmp;
        }

        // Call this if the drawing changes, or you rebuild blocks
        public static void ClearCache() => _iconCache.Clear();
    }
}
```

# 3) Owner-draw ComboBox control (text + image)
```csharp
// v1.0.0 (2025-10-01)
// Purpose: A combo box that draws "icon + text" for block choices.
// Usage: Drop on your palette UserControl and set DataSource to List<BlockItem>.

using System;
using System.Drawing;
using System.Windows.Forms;

namespace AutoCAD.Forms
{
    public class ImageComboBox : ComboBox
    {
        public ImageComboBox()
        {
            DrawMode = DrawMode.OwnerDrawFixed;
            ItemHeight = 36; // nice, roomy row height for 24–32px icons
            DropDownStyle = ComboBoxStyle.DropDownList;
        }

        protected override void OnDrawItem(DrawItemEventArgs e)
        {
            e.DrawBackground();
            if (e.Index < 0)
            {
                base.OnDrawItem(e);
                return;
            }

            var g = e.Graphics;
            var bounds = e.Bounds;
            var item = Items[e.Index] as BlockItem;

            // Layout paddings
            int padX = 6;
            int padY = 4;

            // Icon box
            Rectangle iconRect = new Rectangle(bounds.Left + padX, bounds.Top + padY, ItemHeight - (padY * 2), ItemHeight - (padY * 2));

            // Text box (to the right of icon)
            int textLeft = iconRect.Right + 8;
            Rectangle textRect = new Rectangle(textLeft, bounds.Top, bounds.Width - textLeft - 6, bounds.Height);

            // Draw icon if present
            if (item != null && item.Icon != null)
            {
                // Center icon within iconRect
                var img = item.Icon;
                var x = iconRect.Left + (iconRect.Width - img.Width) / 2;
                var y = iconRect.Top + (iconRect.Height - img.Height) / 2;
                g.DrawImage(img, x, y, img.Width, img.Height);
                // Optional: draw subtle border
                using (var pen = new Pen(Color.FromArgb(60, 60, 60)))
                    g.DrawRectangle(pen, iconRect);
            }

            // Draw text
            using (var brush = new SolidBrush(e.ForeColor))
            using (var format = new StringFormat { LineAlignment = StringAlignment.Center })
            {
                var text = item != null ? item.Name : Convert.ToString(Items[e.Index]);
                g.DrawString(text, e.Font, brush, textRect, format);
            }

            e.DrawFocusRectangle();
            base.OnDrawItem(e);
        }
    }
}
```

# 4) Wiring it into your palette (UserControl)
```csharp
// v1.0.0 (2025-10-01)
// Purpose: Example integration into your existing palette control.

using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Drawing;
using System.Windows.Forms;

namespace AutoCAD.Forms
{
    public partial class TagPaletteControl : UserControl
    {
        private ImageComboBox _cmbBlocks;

        public TagPaletteControl()
        {
            InitializeComponent();
            BuildUi();
            LoadBlocks();
        }

        private void BuildUi()
        {
            _cmbBlocks = new ImageComboBox { Dock = DockStyle.Top };
            Controls.Add(_cmbBlocks);

            // Optional: wire a SelectedIndexChanged to update a larger preview or properties
            _cmbBlocks.SelectedIndexChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                var item = _cmbBlocks.SelectedItem as BlockItem;
                // TODO: update a larger PictureBox preview or enable/disable tag inputs
            };
        }

        private void LoadBlocks()
        {
            // Provide a tiny fallback icon (16–24px). You can embed a resource or make one on the fly.
            Bitmap fallback = CreateFallbackGlyph(20, 20);

            List<BlockItem> items = BlockPreviewService.GetBlockItems(fallback);
            _cmbBlocks.BeginUpdate();
            _cmbBlocks.DataSource = items;   // Owner-draw will render icons + names
            _cmbBlocks.DisplayMember = nameof(BlockItem.Name);
            _cmbBlocks.EndUpdate();
        }

        private static Bitmap CreateFallbackGlyph(int w, int h)
        {
            var bmp = new Bitmap(w, h);
            using (var g = Graphics.FromImage(bmp))
            using (var pen = new Pen(Color.Gray, 2))
            {
                g.Clear(Color.Transparent);
                g.DrawRectangle(pen, 2, 2, w - 4, h - 4);
                g.DrawLine(pen, 4, h - 4, w - 4, 4);
            }
            return bmp;
        }

        // If you reload blocks (e.g., after insertion), call:
        public void RefreshBlockList()
        {
            BlockPreviewService.ClearCache();
            LoadBlocks();
        }
    }
}
```

---

## Notes & Tips

- **Performance:** The preview icon fetch is fast if the block has a stored icon. Caching avoids repeated DB access while the palette is open.
- **When previews are null:** Some blocks won’t have a preview; the fallback glyph keeps the UI consistent. You can also pre-bake **32×32 PNGs** per standard symbol and map by block name (hybrid approach).
- **Bigger preview on hover:** Add a `PictureBox` next to the combo and update it on `SelectedIndexChanged` for a 64–128px preview.
- **Dynamic blocks:** You’ll typically preview the **definition** (not each reference). That’s fine for picking a symbol pattern for tagging.
- **Drawing changes:** If users add/remove block definitions while the palette is open, provide a **Refresh** button that calls `RefreshBlockList()`.

If you want, I can adapt this to your existing **Tag Manager** palette class (namespaces, folder structure, and event hooks you already use), and add a “**Zoom to sample insertion**” context action right from the dropdown selection.

## Response:
10/6/2025, 3:30:35 PM

Gotcha—so after an ESC/cancel, you don’t want the palette to go blank anymore. You want it to snap back to a **“home” view** that shows:

- **Line Label → Next number preview** (e.g., `PR-0125`)
- **Tag Label → Next number preview** (whatever your tag stream is)

Below is a clean way to wire that in (C# 7.3). It keeps your current logic, adds a **Peek** (non-incrementing) call to your number store, and refreshes the palette on **Cancel/End** of commands.

---

# 1) Add a “Peek” to your number store (no increment)
```csharp
// v1.1.0  (2025-10-06)  NodLineNumberStore: add Peek()
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    public static class NodLineNumberStore
    {
        // existing: public static string Next(string scopeKey) { ... } // increments

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the next value WITHOUT incrementing the stored counter.
        /// </summary>
        public static string Peek(string scopeKey)
        {
            // Reuse your existing storage layout; this is identical to Next()
            // except we do NOT write the increment back.
            var db = HostApplicationServices.WorkingDatabase;
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!nod.Contains(scopeKey)) return null;

                var dictId = (ObjectId)nod.GetAt(scopeKey);
                var dict = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(dictId, OpenMode.ForRead);

                // e.g., “Current” or whatever key you use now
                if (!dict.Contains("Current")) return null;

                var xrec = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(dict.GetAt("Current"), OpenMode.ForRead);
                var data = xrec.Data; // ResultBuffer
                // parse your current format (prefix + seq, etc.)
                var value = ParseFromBuffer(data); // <- your existing helper
                // DO NOT increment.
                return value;
            }
        }
    }
}
```

If your next number depends on **prefix** and/or **scope** (Area, Discipline), mirror the signature:
```csharp
public static string Peek(string scopeKey, string prefix);
```

---

# 2) Palette: add a “Home” model + refresh method
```csharp
// v1.1.0  (2025-10-06)  Properties palette "home" labels + refresh
using System.Windows.Forms;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;

namespace AutoCAD.Forms
{
    public partial class CBIPropertiesPalette : UserControl
    {
        // Simple labels at the top of the palette:
        private readonly Label _lblLineNext = new Label { Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true };
        private readonly Label _lblTagNext  = new Label { Dock = DockStyle.Top, AutoSize = true };

        public CBIPropertiesPalette()
        {
            InitializeComponent();

            Controls.Add(_lblTagNext);
            Controls.Add(_lblLineNext);

            // Optional: also keep your existing sections below
            // Controls.Add(_yourOtherGroups...);

            RefreshHomePreview();  // show on startup
        }

        public void RefreshHomePreview()
        {
            // Read current UI selections like Layer/Prefix if needed
            var prefix = GetCurrentPrefixFromUI() ?? "PR-";   // from your “General → Prefix” field
            var lineScope = "LINE";                           // or whichever key you use
            var tagScope  = "TAG";

            var nextLine = NodLineNumberStore.Peek(lineScope /*, prefix */) ?? "(not set)";
            var nextTag  = NodLineNumberStore.Peek(tagScope  /*, prefix */) ?? "(not set)";

            _lblLineNext.Text = $"Line label next: {nextLine}";
            _lblTagNext.Text  = $"Tag label next:  {nextTag}";
        }

        private string GetCurrentPrefixFromUI()
        {
            // If you have a textbox/bound field in the palette, read it here.
            // Example: return txtPrefix.Text;
            return "PR-";
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// When user clicks Apply (or you programmatically commit), call after updating counters.
        /// </summary>
        public void OnApplied()
        {
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// When user clicks Revert/Save or cancels out of a place/refresh command, call this.
        /// </summary>
        public void OnCancelledOrIdle()
        {
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }
    }
}
```

---

# 3) Return to “Home” on ESC/cancel and after commands
Hook two places:

**A) Inside your interactive commands** (line label, refresh label). When a prompt returns `PromptStatus.Cancel`, call the palette’s `OnCancelledOrIdle()`.

```csharp
// v1.1.0  (2025-10-06)  Example inside your command method
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using AcApp = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application;

[CommandMethod("CBI_PlaceLineTag")]
public static void CBI_PlaceLineTag()
{
    var doc = AcApp.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
    var ed  = doc.Editor;

    try
    {
        var peo = new PromptEntityOptions("\nSelect pipe run polyline: ");
        peo.SetRejectMessage("\nMust be a polyline.");
        peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices.Polyline), true);
        var per = ed.GetEntity(peo);

        if (per.Status == PromptStatus.Cancel)
        {
            UI.Palettes.PropertiesPalette?.OnCancelledOrIdle();
            return;
        }

        // ... continue logic ...
        // after successful apply, refresh preview:
        UI.Palettes.PropertiesPalette?.OnApplied();
    }
    catch
    {
        // on error, still return to home view:
        UI.Palettes.PropertiesPalette?.OnCancelledOrIdle();
        throw;
    }
}
```

**B) Globally for any cancel/end**—subscribe once when you load your app:

```csharp
// v1.1.0  (2025-10-06)  Global palette refresh on command cancel/end
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using AcApp = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application;

public static class AppEvents
{
    private static bool _wired;

    public static void Wire()
    {
        if (_wired) return;
        _wired = true;

        AcApp.DocumentManager.DocumentCreated += (_, e) => HookDoc(e.Document);
        foreach (Document d in AcApp.DocumentManager) HookDoc(d);
    }

    private static void HookDoc(Document doc)
    {
        doc.CommandCancelled += (_, __) => UI.Palettes.PropertiesPalette?.OnCancelledOrIdle();
        doc.CommandEnded     += (_, __) => UI.Palettes.PropertiesPalette?.OnCancelledOrIdle();
        // Optional: doc.CommandWillStart += ...
    }
}
```

Call `AppEvents.Wire()` from your initialization (e.g., `IExtensionApplication.Initialize`).

- When you hit **Apply** and increment counters, the **Home** view immediately updates.

## Response:
10/6/2025, 3:38:40 PM

Perfect timing — yes, let’s lock that down cleanly.  
Here’s a **modernized `NodLineNumberStore` static class** (C# 7.3-compliant) designed for your CBI Tag/Line tools in **AutoCAD 2020**.  
It supports both `Next()` and `Peek()` for project-based sequential numbering with prefixes and per-scope dictionaries — no dependency changes needed.

---

### ✅ **File:** `NodLineNumberStore.cs`  
**Namespace:** `AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services`  
**Version:** 1.1.0 (2025-10-06)  
**Purpose:** Centralized sequential numbering stored safely in the Named Objects Dictionary (NOD).

```csharp
using System;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Provides project-based line/tag numbering persisted in AutoCAD's NOD.
    /// Supports per-scope counters, with Peek (read-only) and Next (increment).
    /// </summary>
    public static class NodLineNumberStore
    {
        private const string RootDictName = "CBI_LineTagStore";
        private const string RecordKey = "Current";

        /// <summary>
        /// Retrieves the next available number and increments it.
        /// </summary>
        public static string Next(string scopeKey, string prefix = "")
        {
            var db = HostApplicationServices.WorkingDatabase;
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                // Get or create root dictionary
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                DBDictionary root;
                if (!nod.Contains(RootDictName))
                {
                    nod.UpgradeOpen();
                    root = new DBDictionary();
                    nod.SetAt(RootDictName, root);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootDictName), OpenMode.ForRead);
                }

                // Get or create sub-dictionary per scope (e.g., "LINE", "TAG")
                DBDictionary scopeDict;
                if (!root.Contains(scopeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    scopeDict = new DBDictionary();
                    root.SetAt(scopeKey, scopeDict);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(scopeDict, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    scopeDict = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(scopeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                }

                // Get or create XRecord that holds the counter
                Xrecord rec;
                if (!scopeDict.Contains(RecordKey))
                {
                    scopeDict.UpgradeOpen();
                    rec = new Xrecord();
                    rec.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, 1));
                    scopeDict.SetAt(RecordKey, rec);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(rec, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    rec = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(scopeDict.GetAt(RecordKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                }

                // Extract and increment
                int value = 1;
                if (rec.Data != null)
                {
                    foreach (TypedValue tv in rec.Data)
                    {
                        if (tv.TypeCode == (int)DxfCode.Int32)
                        {
                            value = Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }

                string formatted = $"{prefix}{value:D4}";
                value++;

                // Save new value
                rec.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, value));
                tr.Commit();

                return formatted;
            }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the current next value without incrementing.
        /// </summary>
        public static string Peek(string scopeKey, string prefix = "")
        {
            var db = HostApplicationServices.WorkingDatabase;
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);

                if (!nod.Contains(RootDictName))
                    return $"{prefix}0001"; // default

                var root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootDictName), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!root.Contains(scopeKey))
                    return $"{prefix}0001";

                var scopeDict = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(scopeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!scopeDict.Contains(RecordKey))
                    return $"{prefix}0001";

                var rec = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(scopeDict.GetAt(RecordKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                int value = 1;
                if (rec.Data != null)
                {
                    foreach (TypedValue tv in rec.Data)
                    {
                        if (tv.TypeCode == (int)DxfCode.Int32)
                        {
                            value = Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }

                string formatted = $"{prefix}{value:D4}";
                return formatted;
            }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Resets a given scope counter to a specific value.
        /// </summary>
        public static void Reset(string scopeKey, int startValue = 1)
        {
            var db = HostApplicationServices.WorkingDatabase;
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                DBDictionary root;
                if (!nod.Contains(RootDictName))
                {
                    nod.UpgradeOpen();
                    root = new DBDictionary();
                    nod.SetAt(RootDictName, root);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootDictName), OpenMode.ForRead);
                }

                DBDictionary scopeDict;
                if (!root.Contains(scopeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    scopeDict = new DBDictionary();
                    root.SetAt(scopeKey, scopeDict);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(scopeDict, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    scopeDict = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(scopeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                }

                Xrecord rec;
                if (!scopeDict.Contains(RecordKey))
                {
                    scopeDict.UpgradeOpen();
                    rec = new Xrecord();
                    scopeDict.SetAt(RecordKey, rec);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(rec, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    rec = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(scopeDict.GetAt(RecordKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                }

                rec.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, startValue));
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }
    }
}
```

---

### ⚙️ **Highlights**
| Feature | Description |
|----------|--------------|
| **RootDictName** | `CBI_LineTagStore` under NOD — keeps all project counters together. |
| **ScopeKey** | `"LINE"`, `"TAG"`, `"VALVE"`, etc. — one sub-dictionary per type. |
| **Next()** | Increments and returns formatted string (e.g. `PR-0005`). |
| **Peek()** | Returns the current next value without incrementing. |
| **Reset()** | Allows manual reset or re-numbering start point. |
| **Safe Transactions** | Fully wrapped; creates dictionaries on demand. |
| **Compatible** | AutoCAD 2020 .NET API; C# 7.3 syntax. |

---

### 💡 **Example usage**
```csharp
string nextLine = NodLineNumberStore.Next("LINE", "PR-");  // returns "PR-0001", increments
string preview  = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG",  "T-");   // returns "T-0003" (no increment)
NodLineNumberStore.Reset("TAG", 1);                        // reset tag counter
```

## Response:
10/6/2025, 3:43:14 PM

> **Providing updated class for NodLineNumberStore**
>
> We need to offer an updated version of the `NodLineNumberStore` class to meet the user's requirements, keeping the structure compatible with existing code. We will ensure that the class is sealed, but make methods static, maintaining the same method signatures. I'll add the requested features like `SanitizeKey`, `Next`, and `Prefix` formatting.
>
> Thought for 18s

You’re right to be cautious—let’s keep your existing pattern so nothing breaks.

Below is a **drop-in, backward-compatible** `NodLineNumberStore` that:

- Preserves your **`RootKey = "CBI_LINE_STORE"`** and **`SanitizeKey(string)`**.
- Keeps your original **`Next(string scopeKey) : int`** (returns the raw counter).
- Adds **`PeekValue(string)`** (no increment) and formatted helpers:
  - **`NextFormatted(scope, prefix, width)`**
  - **`Peek(scope, prefix, width)`**
- Includes a **safe Reset**.
- Exposes an **`Instance` adapter** so existing code that uses `ITagNumberingStore` still compiles, while all logic remains static.

### NodLineNumberStore.cs (C# 7.3)

```csharp
// v1.2.0 (2025-10-06)
// Purpose: Safe, backward-compatible line/tag numbering store in NOD.
// Notes:
// - Keeps your RootKey and SanitizeKey behavior.
// - Adds Peek/Formatted helpers without changing your existing Next(int) usage.

using System;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    public sealed class NodLineNumberStore : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        private const string RootKey = "CBI_LINE_STORE";
        private const string RecordKey = "Current";

        // ---- Singleton adapter for ITagNumberingStore (non-breaking) ----
        public static readonly ITagNumberingStore Instance = new StoreAdapter();

        private sealed class StoreAdapter : ITagNumberingStore
        {
            int ITagNumberingStore.Next(string scopeKey) => NodLineNumberStore.Next(scopeKey);
        }

        private NodLineNumberStore() { } // prevent instantiation

        // Allow only letters, digits, underscore, dash, dot; all else -> underscore.
        private static string SanitizeKey(string key)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(key)) return "_";
            var chars = key.ToCharArray();
            for (int i = 0; i < chars.Length; i++)
            {
                char c = chars[i];
                bool ok =
                    (c >= '0' && c <= '9') ||
                    (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z') ||
                    (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') ||
                    c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';
                if (!ok) chars[i] = '_';
            }
            return new string(chars);
        }

        // ------------------ Public API (backward compatible) ------------------

        /// <summary>Gets the next counter value for the given scope and increments it.</summary>
        public static int Next(string scopeKey)
        {
            scopeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);
            var db = HostApplicationServices.WorkingDatabase;

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);
                var scope = GetOrCreateScopeDict(tr, root, scopeKey);

                // xrec holds current int value
                Xrecord rec;
                if (!scope.Contains(RecordKey))
                {
                    scope.UpgradeOpen();
                    rec = new Xrecord { Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, 1)) };
                    scope.SetAt(RecordKey, rec);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(rec, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    rec = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(scope.GetAt(RecordKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                    if (rec.Data == null)
                        rec.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, 1));
                }

                int current = ReadInt(rec.Data, 1);
                int toReturn = current;
                int next = current + 1;

                rec.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, next));
                tr.Commit();

                return toReturn;
            }
        }

        /// <summary>Returns the current "next" value without incrementing.</summary>
        public static int PeekValue(string scopeKey)
        {
            scopeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);
            var db = HostApplicationServices.WorkingDatabase;

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!nod.Contains(RootKey)) return 1;

                var root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!root.Contains(scopeKey)) return 1;

                var scope = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(scopeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!scope.Contains(RecordKey)) return 1;

                var rec = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(scope.GetAt(RecordKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                return ReadInt(rec.Data, 1);
            }
        }

        /// <summary>Formatted, non-incrementing peek (e.g., "PR-0007").</summary>
        public static string Peek(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
        {
            var v = PeekValue(scopeKey);
            return Format(prefix, v, width);
        }

        /// <summary>Formatted, incrementing next (e.g., "PR-0007").</summary>
        public static string NextFormatted(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
        {
            var v = Next(scopeKey);
            return Format(prefix, v, width);
        }

        /// <summary>Resets a scope to a specific start value (default 1).</summary>
        public static void Reset(string scopeKey, int startValue = 1)
        {
            scopeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);
            var db = HostApplicationServices.WorkingDatabase;

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);
                var scope = GetOrCreateScopeDict(tr, root, scopeKey);

                Xrecord rec;
                if (!scope.Contains(RecordKey))
                {
                    scope.UpgradeOpen();
                    rec = new Xrecord();
                    scope.SetAt(RecordKey, rec);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(rec, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    rec = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(scope.GetAt(RecordKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                }

                rec.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, startValue));
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

        // --------------------------- Helpers ----------------------------------

        private static DBDictionary GetOrCreateRootDict(Transaction tr, Database db)
        {
            var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
            if (!nod.Contains(RootKey))
            {
                nod.UpgradeOpen();
                var root = new DBDictionary();
                nod.SetAt(RootKey, root);
                tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                return root;
            }
            return (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
        }

        private static DBDictionary GetOrCreateScopeDict(Transaction tr, DBDictionary root, string scopeKey)
        {
            if (!root.Contains(scopeKey))
            {
                root.UpgradeOpen();
                var scope = new DBDictionary();
                root.SetAt(scopeKey, scope);
                tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(scope, true);
                return scope;
            }
            return (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(scopeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
        }

        private static int ReadInt(ResultBuffer rb, int @default)
        {
            if (rb == null) return @default;
            foreach (TypedValue tv in rb)
                if (tv.TypeCode == (int)DxfCode.Int32)
                    return Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);
            return @default;
        }

        private static string Format(string prefix, int value, int width)
        {
            if (width < 1) width = 1;
            var num = value.ToString("D" + width);
            return string.IsNullOrEmpty(prefix) ? num : (prefix + num);
        }
    }

    // If your ITagNumberingStore has a different signature, adjust here.
    public interface ITagNumberingStore
    {
        int Next(string scopeKey);
    }
}
```

### How to use (unchanged + new)
```csharp
// Backward-compatible usage:
int n1 = NodLineNumberStore.Next("LINE");          // returns 1, then stores 2

// New helpers:
int peekInt = NodLineNumberStore.PeekValue("LINE");                // 2 (no increment)
string preview = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", "PR-", 4);        // "PR-0002"
string nextStr = NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("TAG", "T-", 3); // "T-001"
NodLineNumberStore.Reset("LINE", 1);                               // reset
```

This keeps your **sanitize** logic, avoids API surprises, and gives you the **Peek** + **formatted** strings you need for the palette “home view.” If your `ITagNumberingStore` interface has more members, tell me and I’ll extend the adapter to match exactly.

// File: NodLineNumberStore.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
// Version: 1.0.0
// Changelog:
//  - 1.0.0: Initial NOD/XRecord-backed line-number allocator (scopeKey -> 1..N)

using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Simple per-scope counter stored under NOD/CBI_LINE_STORE.
    /// scopeKey example: "MR|2554|CS1S09"
    /// </summary>
    public sealed class NodLineNumberStore : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        private const string RootKey = "CBI_LINE_STORE";

        // Allow only letters, digits, underscore, dash, dot.
        // Everything else becomes underscore.
        private static string SanitizeKey(string key)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(key)) return "_";
            var chars = key.ToCharArray();
            for (int i = 0; i < chars.Length; i++)
            {
                char c = chars[i];
                bool ok =
                    (c >= '0' && c <= '9') ||
                    (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z') ||
                    (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') ||
                    c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';
                if (!ok) chars[i] = '_';
            }
            return new string(chars);
        }

        public int Next(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 0;
            var db = doc.Database;

            // sanitize here
            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                DBDictionary root;

                if (!nod.Contains(RootKey))
                {
                    nod.UpgradeOpen();
                    root = new DBDictionary();
                    nod.SetAt(RootKey, root);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                }

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord { Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(90, 1)) };
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                    tr.Commit();
                    return 1;
                }
                else
                {
                    xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                    var current = (int)xr.Data.AsArray()[0].Value; // stored "next"
                    xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(90, current + 1));
                    tr.Commit();
                    return current;
                }
            }
        }

}
}

You’re right—your original store is slightly different from the one I proposed. Here’s a clear QC comparison and a **drop-in, fully compatible upgrade** that keeps your original data layout but adds the features you want.

---

# What changed (QC)

**Original (v1.0.0)**
- **Root:** `NOD["CBI_LINE_STORE"]`
- **Storage per scope:** an **Xrecord directly under the root** with key = `SanitizeKey(scopeKey)`
- **Data:** single `Int32` (DXF 90) storing the **next value**  
- **API:** `int Next(string scopeKey)` only (returns current; then increments)
- **Doc/DB:** `Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument` (your preference)
- **Sanitize:** present ✅

**My earlier rewrite (v1.2.0)**
- Introduced **sub-dictionaries per scope** and a `"Current"` record → **layout change** ❗
- Added **Peek/Reset/Formatted** helpers
- Used `HostApplicationServices.WorkingDatabase`

**Risk:** That layout change would break existing counters in drawings.  
**Fix:** Keep your **original layout** (Xrecord per scope under the root dict) and simply add **Peek/Reset/Formatted**. Also keep your **MdiActiveDocument** pattern and your **SanitizeKey**.

---

# ✅ Drop-in replacement (keeps your original layout)

```csharp
// File: NodLineNumberStore.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
// Version: 1.3.0
// Changelog:
//  - 1.0.0: Initial per-scope counter (Xrecord under NOD/CBI_LINE_STORE).
//  - 1.3.0: Adds Peek/Reset + formatted helpers; preserves original storage layout.
//           Uses MdiActiveDocument DB access per team preference.

using System;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions; // keep your existing interface

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Per-scope counter stored in NOD["CBI_LINE_STORE"][safeScopeKey] as a single Int32 (DXF 90).
    /// Next(): returns current then increments the stored "next".
    /// Peek(): returns current "next" without incrementing.
    /// </summary>
    public sealed class NodLineNumberStore : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        private const string RootKey = "CBI_LINE_STORE";

        // Allow only letters, digits, underscore, dash, dot; all else -> underscore.
        private static string SanitizeKey(string key)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(key)) return "_";
            var chars = key.ToCharArray();
            for (int i = 0; i < chars.Length; i++)
            {
                char c = chars[i];
                bool ok =
                    (c >= '0' && c <= '9') ||
                    (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z') ||
                    (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') ||
                    c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';
                if (!ok) chars[i] = '_';
            }
            return new string(chars);
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the current value and increments stored "next".
        /// Layout is unchanged from v1.0.0 for full compatibility.
        /// </summary>
        public int Next(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 0;
            var db = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);
                Xrecord xr;

                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord { Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, 2)) };
                    // We will return 1 (current), and store 2 as next.
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                    tr.Commit();
                    return 1;
                }

                xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                int next = ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
                int current = next;        // value we return now
                int newNext = current + 1; // value to store back
                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, newNext));
                tr.Commit();
                return current;
            }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the current "next" value WITHOUT incrementing (defaults to 1 if missing).
        /// </summary>
        public static int PeekValue(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 1;
            var db = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!nod.Contains(RootKey)) return 1;

                var root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey)) return 1;

                var xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                return ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
            }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Formatted, non-incrementing peek (e.g., "PR-0007").
        /// </summary>
        public static string Peek(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, PeekValue(scopeKey), width);

        /// <summary>
        /// Formatted, incrementing next (e.g., "PR-0007" then store +1).
        /// </summary>
        public static string NextFormatted(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, Next(scopeKey), width);

        /// <summary>
        /// Resets the stored "next" value (defaults to 1).
        /// </summary>
        public static void Reset(string scopeKey, int startValue = 1)
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return;
            var db = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord();
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                }

                // Store the next value directly
                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Int32, startValue));
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

        // ----------------- helpers (unchanged semantics) -----------------

        private static DBDictionary GetOrCreateRootDict(Transaction tr, Database db)
        {
            var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
            if (!nod.Contains(RootKey))
            {
                nod.UpgradeOpen();
                var root = new DBDictionary();
                nod.SetAt(RootKey, root);
                tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                return root;
            }
            return (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
        }

        private static int ReadInt32OrDefault(ResultBuffer rb, int @default)
        {
            if (rb == null) return @default;
            foreach (TypedValue tv in rb)
                if (tv.TypeCode == (int)DxfCode.Int32 || tv.TypeCode == 90)
                    return Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);
            return @default;
        }

        private static string Format(string prefix, int value, int width)
        {
            if (width < 1) width = 1;
            var num = value.ToString("D" + width);
            return string.IsNullOrEmpty(prefix) ? num : prefix + num;
        }
    }
}
```

## Why this is safe

- **Same storage**: `NOD["CBI_LINE_STORE"][safeScopeKey]` → one Xrecord with DXF 90 int.  
- **Same semantics**: `Next(scope)` **returns current** and stores **current+1**.  
- **No migration needed**: Existing drawings keep working.  
- **Adds Peek/Reset/Formatted** for your palette “home view”.

If you want, I can also add a tiny **self-check** method (`bool Exists(scopeKey, out int nextValue)`) or a **`TryGet`** to help with diagnostics.

## Response:

Ah — great catch 👀, and you spotted exactly what Visual Studio was complaining about:  

> **CS0120: “An object reference is required for the non-static field, method, or property ‘NodLineNumberStore.Next(string)’.”**

That means the compiler sees `Next()` as an **instance** member, not static, inside the same static call expression.  

Let’s QC this precisely:

---

### 🧩 Root cause
In your file:
```csharp
public sealed class NodLineNumberStore : ITagNumberingStore
```
The `class` itself is **not static**, and your `Next()` method is **not marked static**, so when `NextFormatted()` tries to call `Next(scopeKey)` without an instance, C# says “I need an object reference.”

---

### ✅ Two possible correct fixes

#### **Option A — make `Next` static**  
This is the correct path for the design we’ve been following (all methods static, stateless store).

```csharp
public static int Next(string scopeKey)
```

Then every other reference (`PeekValue`, `Reset`, etc.) works exactly as written.  
✅  Most consistent with your v1.0.0 code where you called `NodLineNumberStore.Next()` directly.

---

#### **Option B — leave `Next` instance (implements ITagNumberingStore)**
If your interface `ITagNumberingStore` defines `int Next(string scopeKey)` and you must keep it as an instance method, then change `NextFormatted` and any other internal call to use the singleton adapter pattern:

```csharp
public static string NextFormatted(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
    => Format(prefix, Instance.Next(scopeKey), width);
```

…and declare the singleton somewhere in the class:

```csharp
public static readonly NodLineNumberStore Instance = new NodLineNumberStore();
```

This makes your interface happy while letting static helpers delegate to the one shared instance.

---

### ⚙️ Recommended (cleanest + consistent with v1.0.0)

You’ve always used it statically in your tools (`NodLineNumberStore.Next("LINE")`), so use **Option A**.

Here’s the small correction diff:

```diff
- public int Next(string scopeKey)
+ public static int Next(string scopeKey)
```

That’s it — single keyword change, no runtime or data-layout impact.

---

### 🔍 Quick sanity test
After recompiling, this should all compile cleanly:

```csharp
string tagPreview = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG", "PR-", 4);
string nextLine   = NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("LINE", "PR-", 4);
int rawNext       = NodLineNumberStore.Next("VALVE");
```

No more CS0120, and you keep your original 1-up counters intact.

### `NodLineNumberStore.cs` (C# 7.3)

```csharp
// File: NodLineNumberStore.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
// Version: 1.3.1
// Changelog:
//  - 1.0.0: Initial per-scope counter (Xrecord under NOD/CBI_LINE_STORE).
//  - 1.3.0: Added Peek/Reset + formatted helpers; preserved original layout.
//  - 1.3.1: Made Next(string) static; kept ITagNumberingStore via explicit impl; minor safety tweaks.

using System;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions; // ITagNumberingStore

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Per-scope counter stored in NOD["CBI_LINE_STORE"][safeScopeKey] as a single Int32 (DXF 90).
    /// Layout is unchanged from v1.0.0.
    /// - Next(scope): returns current value and persists current+1 as the next.
    /// - Peek*(scope): returns the current "next" without incrementing.
    /// - *Formatted helpers return prefix + zero-padded number for UI.
    /// </summary>
    public sealed class NodLineNumberStore : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        private const string RootKey  = "CBI_LINE_STORE";
        private const int    DxfInt32 = (int)DxfCode.Int32; // 90

        // Prevent external instantiation; interface supported via explicit implementation.
        private NodLineNumberStore() { }

        // ----------------------------- Public API -----------------------------

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the current value and increments the stored "next".
        /// Storage layout and behavior are fully compatible with v1.0.0.
        /// </summary>
        public static int Next(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 0;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    // First allocation for this scope: return 1, store 2 as next.
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord { Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, 2)) };
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                    tr.Commit();
                    return 1;
                }

                xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                var next = ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
                var current = next;           // to return
                var newNext = current + 1;    // to persist
                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, newNext));
                tr.Commit();
                return current;
            }
        }

        /// <summary>Returns the current "next" value WITHOUT incrementing (defaults to 1 if missing).</summary>
        public static int PeekValue(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 1;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!nod.Contains(RootKey)) return 1;

                var root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey)) return 1;

                var xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                return ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
            }
        }

        /// <summary>Formatted, non-incrementing peek (e.g., "PR-0007").</summary>
        public static string Peek(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, PeekValue(scopeKey), width);

        /// <summary>Formatted, incrementing next (e.g., "PR-0007" and then store +1).</summary>
        public static string NextFormatted(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, Next(scopeKey), width);

        /// <summary>Resets the stored "next" value for a scope (defaults to 1).</summary>
        public static void Reset(string scopeKey, int startValue = 1)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord();
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                }

                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, startValue));
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

        // ------------------------ ITagNumberingStore -------------------------
        // Keep compatibility with any places that expect an instance via DI.
        int ITagNumberingStore.Next(string scopeKey) => Next(scopeKey);

        // ------------------------------ Helpers ------------------------------

        // Allow only letters, digits, underscore, dash, dot; everything else becomes underscore.
        private static string SanitizeKey(string key)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(key)) return "_";
            var chars = key.ToCharArray();
            for (int i = 0; i < chars.Length; i++)
            {
                char c = chars[i];
                bool ok =
                    (c >= '0' && c <= '9') ||
                    (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z') ||
                    (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') ||
                    c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';
                if (!ok) chars[i] = '_';
            }
            return new string(chars);
        }

        private static DBDictionary GetOrCreateRootDict(Transaction tr, Database db)
        {
            var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
            if (!nod.Contains(RootKey))
            {
                nod.UpgradeOpen();
                var root = new DBDictionary();
                nod.SetAt(RootKey, root);
                tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                return root;
            }
            return (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
        }

        private static int ReadInt32OrDefault(ResultBuffer rb, int @default)
        {
            if (rb == null) return @default;
            foreach (TypedValue tv in rb)
            {
                // DXF 90 and DxfCode.Int32 map to the same integer content here.
                if (tv.TypeCode == DxfInt32 || tv.TypeCode == 90)
                    return Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);
            }
            return @default;
        }

        private static string Format(string prefix, int value, int width)
        {
            if (width < 1) width = 1;
            var num = value.ToString("D" + width);
            return string.IsNullOrEmpty(prefix) ? num : prefix + num;
        }
    }
}
```

**How to use (unchanged + new):**
```csharp

// New helpers for your palette home view:

```

You’re getting CS0122 because my last version made the constructor **private** while your code does `new NodLineNumberStore()`. Here’s a **drop-in fix**: same storage/layout as yours, `Next(string)` stays **static**, and the **constructor is public** so your existing `new NodLineNumberStore()` calls compile. It also keeps `ITagNumberingStore` via explicit impl and includes `Peek/Reset` + formatted helpers.

### NodLineNumberStore.cs (v1.3.2, C# 7.3)
```csharp
// File: NodLineNumberStore.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
// Version: 1.3.2
// Changelog:
//  - 1.0.0: Initial per-scope counter (Xrecord under NOD/CBI_LINE_STORE).
//  - 1.3.0: Added Peek/Reset + formatted helpers; preserved original layout.
//  - 1.3.1: Made Next(string) static; explicit ITagNumberingStore impl.
//  - 1.3.2: Constructor made PUBLIC to allow `new NodLineNumberStore()` (fix CS0122).

using System;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions; // ITagNumberingStore

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Per-scope counter stored in NOD["CBI_LINE_STORE"][safeScopeKey] as a single Int32 (DXF 90).
    /// Layout is unchanged from v1.0.0.
    /// - Next(scope): returns current value and persists current+1 as the next.
    /// - Peek*(scope): returns the current "next" without incrementing.
    /// - *Formatted helpers return prefix + zero-padded number for UI.
    /// </summary>
    public sealed class NodLineNumberStore : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        private const string RootKey  = "CBI_LINE_STORE";
        private const int    DxfInt32 = (int)DxfCode.Int32; // 90

        // PUBLIC so existing code that does `new NodLineNumberStore()` compiles.
        public NodLineNumberStore() { }

        // ----------------------------- Public API -----------------------------

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the current value and increments the stored "next".
        /// Storage layout and behavior are fully compatible with v1.0.0.
        /// </summary>
        public static int Next(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 0;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    // First allocation for this scope: return 1, store 2 as next.
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord { Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, 2)) };
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                    tr.Commit();
                    return 1;
                }

                xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                var next    = ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
                var current = next;           // to return
                var newNext = current + 1;    // to persist
                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, newNext));
                tr.Commit();
                return current;
            }
        }

        /// <summary>Returns the current "next" value WITHOUT incrementing (defaults to 1 if missing).</summary>
        public static int PeekValue(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 1;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!nod.Contains(RootKey)) return 1;

                var root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey)) return 1;

                var xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                return ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
            }
        }

        /// <summary>Formatted, non-incrementing peek (e.g., "PR-0007").</summary>
        public static string Peek(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, PeekValue(scopeKey), width);

        /// <summary>Formatted, incrementing next (e.g., "PR-0007" and then store +1).</summary>
        public static string NextFormatted(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, Next(scopeKey), width);

        /// <summary>Resets the stored "next" value for a scope (defaults to 1).</summary>
        public static void Reset(string scopeKey, int startValue = 1)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord();
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                }

                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, startValue));
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

        // ------------------------ ITagNumberingStore -------------------------
        // Explicit implementation so DI expecting an instance still works.
        int ITagNumberingStore.Next(string scopeKey) => Next(scopeKey);

        // ------------------------------ Helpers ------------------------------

        // Allow only letters, digits, underscore, dash, dot; everything else becomes underscore.
        private static string SanitizeKey(string key)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(key)) return "_";
            var chars = key.ToCharArray();
            for (int i = 0; i < chars.Length; i++)
            {
                char c = chars[i];
                bool ok =
                    (c >= '0' && c <= '9') ||
                    (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z') ||
                    (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') ||
                    c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';
                if (!ok) chars[i] = '_';
            }
            return new string(chars);
        }

        private static DBDictionary GetOrCreateRootDict(Transaction tr, Database db)
        {
            var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
            if (!nod.Contains(RootKey))
            {
                nod.UpgradeOpen();
                var root = new DBDictionary();
                nod.SetAt(RootKey, root);
                tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                return root;
            }
            return (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
        }

        private static int ReadInt32OrDefault(ResultBuffer rb, int @default)
        {
            if (rb == null) return @default;
            foreach (TypedValue tv in rb)
            {
                if (tv.TypeCode == DxfInt32 || tv.TypeCode == 90)
                    return Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);
            }
            return @default;
        }

        private static string Format(string prefix, int value, int width)
        {
            if (width < 1) width = 1;
            var num = value.ToString("D" + width);
            return string.IsNullOrEmpty(prefix) ? num : prefix + num;
        }
    }
}
```

- Your existing calls like:
  ```csharp
  var svc = new LineTagServiceCore(new NodLineNumberStore(), ...);
  ```
  will work, and anywhere you want formatted strings for the palette, use:
  ```csharp
  var preview = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", "PR-", 4);
  ```

If you prefer to avoid constructing this at all, we can also add `public static readonly NodLineNumberStore Instance = new NodLineNumberStore();` and switch your `new NodLineNumberStore()` usages to `NodLineNumberStore.Instance`.

> Thought for 22s

No worries — those 52 errors are almost certainly from **duplicate class definitions** of `NodLineNumberStore` in your project.

### What the errors mean
- **CS0111 “already defines a member …”**  
  → You have **two methods with the same signature** (e.g., two `GetOrCreateRootDict(...)`) because **two copies of the class** are being compiled.
- **CS0229 “Ambiguity between … DxfInt32 …”**  
  → The field `DxfInt32` exists **in two different class copies**.
- **CS8626 “explicitly implemented more than once”**  
  → The explicit interface method `ITagNumberingStore.Next(string)` exists **twice** (again, two class copies).

Your screenshot shows filenames like `NodLineNumber...2.cs`, which is a giveaway that you’ve got **multiple files** with the same class and namespace.

---

## Quick Fix (2 minutes)

1. **Find all copies**  
   - In Visual Studio: `Ctrl+T` (or `Ctrl+;`) → search: `class NodLineNumberStore`  
   - Or Solution Explorer search: `NodLineNumberStore.cs`
2. **Keep only ONE file** that defines `AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services.NodLineNumberStore`.  
   - Delete/Exclude any duplicates (e.g., `NodLineNumberStore (2).cs`, old backups, or mistakenly added files).  
   - If you want to preserve an old version, rename it to something else **and** change its class name/namespace so it doesn’t compile (or right-click → Exclude From Project).
3. **Clean & Rebuild** the solution.

That should drop the error count to zero (or back to any genuine compile issues).

---

```csharp
// File: NodLineNumberStore.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
// Version: 1.3.2
// Changelog:
//  - 1.0.0: Initial per-scope counter (Xrecord under NOD/CBI_LINE_STORE).
//  - 1.3.0: Added Peek/Reset + formatted helpers; preserved original layout.
//  - 1.3.2: Public ctor (for `new NodLineNumberStore()`), static Next(string), explicit I/F impl.

using System;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions; // ITagNumberingStore

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Per-scope counter stored in NOD["CBI_LINE_STORE"][safeScopeKey] as a single Int32 (DXF 90).
    /// Layout unchanged from v1.0.0.
    /// - Next(scope): returns current value and persists current+1 as the next.
    /// - Peek*(scope): returns the current "next" without incrementing.
    /// - Formatted helpers return prefix + zero-padded number for UI.
    /// </summary>
    public sealed class NodLineNumberStore : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        private const string RootKey  = "CBI_LINE_STORE";
        private const int    DxfInt32 = (int)DxfCode.Int32; // 90

        // Public so existing code `new NodLineNumberStore()` compiles.
        public NodLineNumberStore() { }

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the current value and increments the stored "next".
        /// Fully compatible with v1.0.0 storage/behavior.
        /// </summary>
        public static int Next(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 0;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    // First allocation: return 1, store 2 as next.
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord { Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, 2)) };
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                    tr.Commit();
                    return 1;
                }

                xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                var next    = ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
                var current = next;           // value to return
                var newNext = current + 1;    // value to persist
                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, newNext));
                tr.Commit();
                return current;
            }
        }

        /// <summary>Returns the current "next" value WITHOUT incrementing (defaults to 1 if missing).</summary>
        public static int PeekValue(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 1;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!nod.Contains(RootKey)) return 1;

                var root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey)) return 1;

                var xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                return ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
            }
        }

        /// <summary>Formatted, non-incrementing peek (e.g., "PR-0007").</summary>
        public static string Peek(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, PeekValue(scopeKey), width);

        /// <summary>Formatted, incrementing next (e.g., "PR-0007" and then store +1).</summary>
        public static string NextFormatted(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, Next(scopeKey), width);

        /// <summary>Resets the stored "next" value for a scope (defaults to 1).</summary>
        public static void Reset(string scopeKey, int startValue = 1)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord();
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                }

                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, startValue));
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

        // Explicit interface implementation for any code expecting an instance.
        int ITagNumberingStore.Next(string scopeKey) => Next(scopeKey);

        // Helpers
        private static string SanitizeKey(string key)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(key)) return "_";
            var chars = key.ToCharArray();
            for (int i = 0; i < chars.Length; i++)
            {
                char c = chars[i];
                bool ok =
                    (c >= '0' && c <= '9') ||
                    (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z') ||
                    (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') ||
                    c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';
                if (!ok) chars[i] = '_';
            }
            return new string(chars);
        }

        private static DBDictionary GetOrCreateRootDict(Transaction tr, Database db)
        {
            var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
            if (!nod.Contains(RootKey))
            {
                nod.UpgradeOpen();
                var root = new DBDictionary();
                nod.SetAt(RootKey, root);
                tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                return root;
            }
            return (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
        }

        private static int ReadInt32OrDefault(ResultBuffer rb, int @default)
        {
            if (rb == null) return @default;
            foreach (TypedValue tv in rb)
            {
                if (tv.TypeCode == DxfInt32 || tv.TypeCode == 90)
                    return Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);
            }
            return @default;
        }

        private static string Format(string prefix, int value, int width)
        {
            if (width < 1) width = 1;
            var num = value.ToString("D" + width);
            return string.IsNullOrEmpty(prefix) ? num : prefix + num;
        }
    }
}
```

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{

        int ITagNumberingStore.Next(string scopeKey) => Next(scopeKey);

        private static string SanitizeKey(string key)

                    (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') ||
                    c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';
                if (!ok) chars[i] = '_';
            }
            return new string(chars);
        }

        private static DBDictionary GetOrCreateRootDict(Transaction tr, Database db)
        {
            var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
            if (!nod.Contains(RootKey))
            {
                nod.UpgradeOpen();
                var root = new DBDictionary();
                nod.SetAt(RootKey, root);
                tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                return root;
            }
            return (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);

        {
            if (rb == null) return @default;
            foreach (TypedValue tv in rb)
            {
                if (tv.TypeCode == DxfInt32 || tv.TypeCode == 90)
                    return Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);

            return @default;

        private static string Format(string prefix, int value, int width)
        {
            if (width < 1) width = 1;
            var num = value.ToString("D" + width);
            return string.IsNullOrEmpty(prefix) ? num : prefix + num;
        }
