## Response:
10/6/2025, 4:07:50 PM

> **Thinking longer for a better answer**
>
> 
>
> Thought for 7s

You’re not crazy—there *are* duplicates. You’ve got **numbering helpers living in two places**:

1) `AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services.NodLineNumberStore` (the class we just finalized)  
2) `SmartLabelServices` (has its own `Peek`, maybe its own `SanitizeKey`, etc.)

That overlap is what’s causing the confusion. Let’s make it clean and single-sourced.

# What to keep vs. remove

- **KEEP** all numbering logic (Next/Peek/Reset/formatting + SanitizeKey) **only in** `NodLineNumberStore`.
- **REMOVE or replace** any similarly named helpers in `SmartLabelServices` that do numbering or sanitizing.

# How to fix SmartLabelServices (surgical edits)

In `SmartLabelServices`:

1) **Delete/Comment** any of these if present:
   - `int PeekValue(string scopeKey)` or `string Peek(...)`
   - `int Next(...)` (if it’s doing NOD/Xrecord work)
   - `string SanitizeKey(string)`
   - Any local `GetOrCreateRootDict`, `ReadInt32OrDefault`, etc.

2) **Replace calls** with the centralized store:

```csharp
// BEFORE (examples)
var nextInt   = PeekValue("LINE");                     // or a local method
var nextStr   = Peek("LINE", prefix, width);
var current   = Next("TAG");
var cleanKey  = SanitizeKey(scope);

// AFTER
var nextInt   = NodLineNumberStore.PeekValue("LINE");
var nextStr   = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", prefix, width);
var current   = NodLineNumberStore.Next("TAG");
var cleanKey  = /* if you still need this locally, call: */ 
                // (keep sanitizing only inside NodLineNumberStore if possible)
                // NodLineNumberStore exposes SanitizeKey as private, so:
                // -> Prefer passing raw scope strings to the store and let it sanitize.
                // If you truly need it outside: copy the 8-line sanitize into a NEW name, e.g. LocalSanitize().
```

3) If some code in `SmartLabelServices` **must** build a formatted preview without incrementing:
```csharp
var preview = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", prefix, 4); // e.g., “PR-0007”
```

4) If some code increments:
```csharp
var tagText = NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("TAG", prefix, 4);
```

# Why this helps
- One source of truth -> no drift, no “which Peek are we using?” moments.
- The store already handles **sanitizing**, **DXF 90**, **doc/db** access, and **layout** compatible with v1.0.0.

# Quick sanity checklist
- [ ] Only one `NodLineNumberStore` class file in the project.
- [ ] `SmartLabelServices` no longer defines `Peek`, `Next`, or `SanitizeKey` that shadow the store.
- [ ] All numbering calls in the app route to `NodLineNumberStore.*`.
- [ ] Build → no CS0111/CS0229/CS8626 duplicates.

Where you build/ensure the label text:

```csharp
// Example usage inside SmartLabelServices when you need a preview for the palette:
string prefix = "PR-"; // read from your palette field
string linePreview = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", prefix, 4);

// When you actually commit and want to consume the next value:
string lineNumber = NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("LINE", prefix, 4);
```

- **Removes** any duplicate numbering helpers (`Peek`, `SanitizeKey`, etc.) from this class.
- **Centralizes numbering** through your finalized `NodLineNumberStore` (static):  
  `Peek/PeekValue/Next/NextFormatted/Reset`.
- Works with **DBText**, **MText**, and **BlockReference attribute** targets.
- Uses your preferred `Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument`.

### `SmartLabelServices.cs` (C# 7.3)

```csharp
// File: SmartLabelServices.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
// Version: 1.0.0 (2025-10-06)
// Changelog:
//  - 1.0.0: New, numbering logic removed from this class. All counters use NodLineNumberStore.
//            Adds helpers to preview and apply line/tag labels to DBText/MText/Attributes.
//
// Notes:
//  - This class intentionally contains no SanitizeKey/PeekValue/Next storage logic.
//    Use NodLineNumberStore for all numbering operations to avoid duplication.
//  - Targets: DBText, MText, BlockReference attribute by tag name.
//  - Prefix/width/autoincrement come from your palette; pass them into the methods below.

using System;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    public sealed class SmartLabelServices
    {
        // ------------------------------- API --------------------------------

        /// <summary>
        /// Non-incrementing preview for the next LINE label (e.g., "PR-0007").
        /// </summary>
        public string PeekLinePreview(string prefix, int width = 4)
            => NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", prefix ?? string.Empty, width);

        /// <summary>
        /// Non-incrementing preview for the next TAG label (e.g., "T-0007").
        /// </summary>
        public string PeekTagPreview(string prefix, int width = 4)
            => NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG", prefix ?? string.Empty, width);

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the next LINE label and increments the counter.
        /// </summary>
        public string NextLineLabel(string prefix, int width = 4)
            => NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("LINE", prefix ?? string.Empty, width);

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns the next TAG label and increments the counter.
        /// </summary>
        public string NextTagLabel(string prefix, int width = 4)
            => NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("TAG", prefix ?? string.Empty, width);

        /// <summary>
        /// Ensures text content for a target entity (DBText/MText/Block attribute).
        /// If empty or whitespace, writes preview or next value depending on <paramref name="autoIncrement"/>.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="targetId">DBText / MText / BlockReference (when using attributeTag)</param>
        /// <param name="attributeTag">
        /// Optional: if targetId is a BlockReference and you want a specific attribute written, supply the tag (case-insensitive).
        /// Leave null/empty to write nothing on BlockReference.
        /// </param>
        /// <param name="isLineLabel">true = use LINE counter, false = use TAG counter</param>
        /// <param name="prefix">Prefix for formatted label (e.g., "PR-")</param>
        /// <param name="width">Zero-pad width (e.g., 4 => 0007)</param>
        /// <param name="autoIncrement">If true, consume the next value; if false, only preview value is written when blank</param>
        /// <param name="changed">Outputs true if we wrote content</param>
        /// <returns>The text that the entity ends up with (or preview if unchanged)</returns>
        public string EnsureLabelText(
            ObjectId targetId,
            string attributeTag,
            bool isLineLabel,
            string prefix,
            int width,
            bool autoIncrement,
            out bool changed)
        {
            changed = false;

            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return string.Empty;
            var db = doc.Database;
            var ed = doc.Editor;

            using (doc.LockDocument())
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var obj = tr.GetObject(targetId, OpenMode.ForRead, false);
                string existing = ReadText(obj, tr, attributeTag);

                // Determine source (LINE/TAG) and value
                var src = isLineLabel ? "LINE" : "TAG";
                string preview = NodLineNumberStore.Peek(src, prefix ?? string.Empty, width);

                // If something is already there, keep it and just return it.
                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(existing))
                    return existing;

                // Nothing there; decide whether to consume or just preview
                string final = autoIncrement
                    ? NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted(src, prefix ?? string.Empty, width)
                    : preview;

                // Write back
                if (WriteText(obj, tr, attributeTag, final))
                {
                    changed = true;
                }

                tr.Commit();
                return final;
            }
        }

        // ----------------------- Selection conveniences ----------------------

        /// <summary>
        /// Prompts for an entity and applies EnsureLabelText to it.
        /// Useful for manual ops or debugging.
        /// </summary>
        [CommandMethod("CBI_SMART_ENSURE_LABEL")]
        public void CmdEnsureLabelInteractive()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return;
            var ed = doc.Editor;

            // Simple entity pick
            var peo = new PromptEntityOptions("\nSelect DBText/MText/Block with attribute to label:");
            peo.SetRejectMessage("\nMust be DBText, MText, or BlockReference.");
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(DBText), true);
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(MText), true);
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(BlockReference), true);

            var per = ed.GetEntity(peo);
            if (per.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            // Minimal demo parameters; wire real values from palette in your app:
            string prefix = "PR-";
            int width = 4;
            bool isLineLabel = true;
            bool autoIncrement = true;
            string attributeTag = "TAG"; // if a block attribute (case-insensitive). Change to your app's tag.

            bool changed;
            string result = EnsureLabelText(
                per.ObjectId, attributeTag, isLineLabel,
                prefix, width, autoIncrement, out changed);

            ed.WriteMessage($"\nLabel {(changed ? "applied" : "previewed")}: {result}");
        }

        // --------------------------- I/O helpers -----------------------------

        private static string ReadText(DBObject obj, Transaction tr, string attributeTag)
        {
            if (obj is DBText dbt)
                return dbt.TextString;

            if (obj is MText mt)
                return mt.Contents;

            if (obj is BlockReference br)
            {
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(attributeTag))
                    return string.Empty;

                var tag = attributeTag.Trim();
                foreach (ObjectId arId in br.AttributeCollection)
                {
                    var ar = tr.GetObject(arId, OpenMode.ForRead) as AttributeReference;
                    if (ar == null) continue;
                    if (string.Equals(ar.Tag, tag, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                        return ar.TextString;
                }
                return string.Empty;
            }

            return string.Empty;
        }

        private static bool WriteText(DBObject obj, Transaction tr, string attributeTag, string value)
        {
            if (obj is DBText dbt)
            {
                dbt.UpgradeOpen();
                dbt.TextString = value ?? string.Empty;
                return true;
            }

            if (obj is MText mt)
            {
                mt.UpgradeOpen();
                mt.Contents = value ?? string.Empty;
                return true;
            }

            if (obj is BlockReference br && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(attributeTag))
            {
                var tag = attributeTag.Trim();
                foreach (ObjectId arId in br.AttributeCollection)
                {
                    var ar = tr.GetObject(arId, OpenMode.ForWrite) as AttributeReference;
                    if (ar == null) continue;
                    if (string.Equals(ar.Tag, tag, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                    {
                        ar.TextString = value ?? string.Empty;
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            return false;
        }

        // -------------------- (other app-specific helpers here…) --------------
    }
}
```

---

## How to wire it

- In your **palette Apply**:
  ```csharp
  var svc = new SmartLabelServices();
  bool changed;
  // example for a DBText or Block attribute you’re targeting:
  string final = svc.EnsureLabelText(
      targetId: entityId,
      attributeTag: "TAG",     // for BlockReference attribute; or null for DBText/MText
      isLineLabel: true,       // true => LINE counter, false => TAG counter
      prefix: txtPrefix.Text,  // from your palette
      width: 4,
      autoIncrement: chkAutoIncrement.Checked,
      out changed
  );
  ```

- For your **palette home view** previews:
  ```csharp
  var svc = new SmartLabelServices();
  lblLineNext.Text = $"Line label next: {svc.PeekLinePreview(txtPrefix.Text, 4)}";
  lblTagNext.Text  = $"Tag label next:  {svc.PeekTagPreview(txtPrefix.Text, 4)}";
  ```

This keeps `SmartLabelServices` focused on **app logic and entity I/O**, while **all numbering** lives in `NodLineNumberStore`. If you paste your previous `SmartLabelServices` here, I can also **map old calls → new ones** line-by-line.

## 1) `PropertiesPalette.cs`

```csharp
// File: PropertiesPalette.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.UI
// Purpose: Single palette set that hosts CustomPropertiesUserControl.

using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Windows;

namespace AutoCAD2020.UI
{
    public static class PropertiesPalette
    {
        private static PaletteSet _ps;
        private static CustomPropertiesUserControl _ui;

        public static CustomPropertiesUserControl UI => _ui;

        public static void Show()
        {
            if (_ps == null)
            {
                _ps = new PaletteSet("CBI Properties", "CBI_Properties_Palette")
                {
                    Visible = true,
                    DockEnabled = (DockSides)(DockSides.Left | DockSides.Right),
                };

                _ui = new CustomPropertiesUserControl();
                _ps.Add("Properties", _ui);
            }
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        public static void RefreshHome()
        {
            _ui?.RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Call when a command ends/cancels so the palette returns to the home preview.
        /// </summary>
        public static void OnCancelledOrIdle()
        {
            _ui?.OnCancelledOrIdle();
        }
    }
}
```

## 2) `CustomPropertiesUserControl.cs`

```csharp
// File: CustomPropertiesUserControl.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.UI
// Purpose: Minimal “Properties” palette UI with Apply/Revert/Save and live previews.

using System;
using System.Drawing;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services; // NodLineNumberStore + SmartLabelServices

namespace AutoCAD2020.UI
{
    public sealed class CustomPropertiesUserControl : UserControl
    {
        // Top command bar
        private readonly Button btnApply  = new Button { Text = "Apply"  };
        private readonly Button btnRevert = new Button { Text = "Revert" };
        private readonly Button btnSave   = new Button { Text = "Save"   };

        // Groups
        private readonly GroupBox grpAppearance = new GroupBox { Text = "Appearance" };
        private readonly GroupBox grpBehavior   = new GroupBox { Text = "Behavior" };
        private readonly GroupBox grpGeneral    = new GroupBox { Text = "General" };

        // Appearance controls (simplified)
        private readonly TextBox txtLayer      = new TextBox { Text = "C-ANNO-TAG" };
        private readonly TextBox txtTextHeight = new TextBox { Text = "0.125" };

        // Behavior controls
        private readonly CheckBox chkAutoIncrement = new CheckBox { Text = "AutoIncrement", Checked = true };

        // General controls
        private readonly TextBox txtPrefix = new TextBox { Text = "PR-" };

        // Preview labels (home view)
        private readonly Label lblLineNext = new Label { AutoSize = true, Font = new Font("Segoe UI", 9F, FontStyle.Regular) };
        private readonly Label lblTagNext  = new Label { AutoSize = true, Font = new Font("Segoe UI", 9F, FontStyle.Regular) };

        private readonly SmartLabelServices _svc = new SmartLabelServices();

        public CustomPropertiesUserControl()
        {
            BuildLayout();
            WireEvents();

            // Initial preview
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        private void BuildLayout()
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
            Padding = new Padding(10);

            var cmdPanel = new FlowLayoutPanel
            {
                Dock = DockStyle.Top,
                Height = 36,
                FlowDirection = FlowDirection.LeftToRight
            };
            cmdPanel.Controls.Add(btnApply);
            cmdPanel.Controls.Add(btnRevert);
            cmdPanel.Controls.Add(btnSave);

            // Appearance layout
            var lay1 = new TableLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Fill, ColumnCount = 2, AutoSize = true };
            lay1.Controls.Add(new Label { Text = "Layer", AutoSize = true }, 0, 0);
            lay1.Controls.Add(txtLayer, 1, 0);
            lay1.Controls.Add(new Label { Text = "TextHeight", AutoSize = true }, 0, 1);
            lay1.Controls.Add(txtTextHeight, 1, 1);
            grpAppearance.Controls.Add(lay1);
            grpAppearance.Dock = DockStyle.Top;

            // Behavior layout
            var lay2 = new FlowLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Fill, AutoSize = true };
            lay2.Controls.Add(chkAutoIncrement);
            grpBehavior.Controls.Add(lay2);
            grpBehavior.Dock = DockStyle.Top;

            // General layout
            var lay3 = new TableLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Fill, ColumnCount = 2, AutoSize = true };
            lay3.Controls.Add(new Label { Text = "Prefix", AutoSize = true }, 0, 0);
            lay3.Controls.Add(txtPrefix, 1, 0);
            grpGeneral.Controls.Add(lay3);
            grpGeneral.Dock = DockStyle.Top;

            // Preview panel (home view)
            var preview = new TableLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, ColumnCount = 1, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(4, 8, 4, 4) };
            preview.Controls.Add(lblLineNext, 0, 0);
            preview.Controls.Add(lblTagNext,  0, 1);

            // Stack controls
            var stack = new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Fill, AutoScroll = true };
            stack.Controls.Add(preview);
            stack.Controls.Add(grpGeneral);
            stack.Controls.Add(grpBehavior);
            stack.Controls.Add(grpAppearance);
            Controls.Add(stack);
            Controls.Add(cmdPanel);
        }

        private void WireEvents()
        {
            btnApply.Click  += (s, e) => OnApply();
            btnRevert.Click += (s, e) => OnRevert();
            btnSave.Click   += (s, e) => OnSave();

            // Live preview changes when prefix toggles
            txtPrefix.TextChanged += (s, e) => RefreshHomePreview();
            chkAutoIncrement.CheckedChanged += (s, e) => RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        // ---------------------- Core palette actions ----------------------

        private string Prefix => txtPrefix.Text ?? string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Refreshes the “home” preview (non-incrementing).</summary>
        public void RefreshHomePreview()
        {
            // Non-incrementing previews:
            lblLineNext.Text = $"Line label next: {NodLineNumberStore.Peek(\"LINE\", Prefix, 4)}";
            lblTagNext.Text  = $"Tag label next:  {NodLineNumberStore.Peek(\"TAG\",  Prefix, 4)}";
        }

        /// <summary>Called by global hooks when commands end/cancel.</summary>
        public void OnCancelledOrIdle()
        {
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        /// <summary>Apply: consume next numbers if AutoIncrement is true; otherwise no increment.</summary>
        private void OnApply()
        {
            if (chkAutoIncrement.Checked)
            {
                // Consume a number each for demonstration.
                // In your real flow, call SmartLabelServices.EnsureLabelText(...) on actual targets.
                var consumedLine = NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("LINE", Prefix, 4);
                var consumedTag  = NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("TAG",  Prefix, 4);

                // Optional: feedback in command line
                var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
                doc?.Editor?.WriteMessage($"\nApplied LINE: {consumedLine}, TAG: {consumedTag}");
            }

            RefreshHomePreview(); // Show the new “next”
        }

        /// <summary>Revert: do not increment; simply reload previews (and you might reload UI state).</summary>
        private void OnRevert()
        {
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        /// <summary>Save: here you would persist palette settings (layer, text height, prefix) to JSON/settings.</summary>
        private void OnSave()
        {
            // TODO: persist to your settings store; for now just acknowledge.
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            doc?.Editor?.WriteMessage("\nCBI Properties: settings saved (placeholder).");
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }
    }
}
```

## 3) `PluginEntry.cs` (init & command)

```csharp
// File: PluginEntry.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020
// Purpose: Initialize palette and wire global command-end/cancel callbacks.

using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;
using AutoCAD2020.UI;

[assembly: CommandClass(typeof(AutoCAD2020.PluginEntry))]

namespace AutoCAD2020
{
    public class PluginEntry : IExtensionApplication
    {
        public void Initialize()
        {
            // Hook existing documents and new ones to refresh palette on cancel/end
            var mgr = Application.DocumentManager;
            foreach (Document d in mgr) HookDoc(d);
            mgr.DocumentCreated += (s, e) => HookDoc(e.Document);
        }

        private static void HookDoc(Document doc)
        {
            doc.CommandCancelled += (s, e) => PropertiesPalette.OnCancelledOrIdle();
            doc.CommandEnded     += (s, e) => PropertiesPalette.OnCancelledOrIdle();
        }

        public void Terminate() { }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROPERTIES")]
        public void CmdShowPropertiesPalette()
        {
            PropertiesPalette.Show();
        }
    }
}
```

# 1) `NodLineNumberStore.cs`  (keep as we finalized)

```csharp
// File: NodLineNumberStore.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
using System;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    public sealed class NodLineNumberStore : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        private const string RootKey  = "CBI_LINE_STORE";
        private const int    DxfInt32 = (int)DxfCode.Int32;

        public NodLineNumberStore() { }

        public static int Next(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 0;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord { Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, 2)) };
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                    tr.Commit();
                    return 1;
                }

                xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                var next    = ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
                var current = next;
                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, current + 1));
                tr.Commit();
                return current;
            }
        }

        public static int PeekValue(string scopeKey)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return 1;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!nod.Contains(RootKey)) return 1;

                var root = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey)) return 1;

                var xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
                return ReadInt32OrDefault(xr.Data, 1);
            }
        }

        public static string Peek(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, PeekValue(scopeKey), width);

        public static string NextFormatted(string scopeKey, string prefix = "", int width = 4)
            => Format(prefix, Next(scopeKey), width);

        public static void Reset(string scopeKey, int startValue = 1)
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null) return;
            var db  = doc.Database;

            var safeKey = SanitizeKey(scopeKey);

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var root = GetOrCreateRootDict(tr, db);

                Xrecord xr;
                if (!root.Contains(safeKey))
                {
                    root.UpgradeOpen();
                    xr = new Xrecord();
                    root.SetAt(safeKey, xr);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(xr, true);
                }
                else
                {
                    xr = (Xrecord)tr.GetObject(root.GetAt(safeKey), OpenMode.ForWrite);
                }

                xr.Data = new ResultBuffer(new TypedValue(DxfInt32, startValue));
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

        int ITagNumberingStore.Next(string scopeKey) => Next(scopeKey);

        private static string SanitizeKey(string key)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(key)) return "_";
            var chars = key.ToCharArray();
            for (int i = 0; i < chars.Length; i++)
            {
                char c = chars[i];
                bool ok =
                    (c >= '0' && c <= '9') ||
                    (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z') ||
                    (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') ||
                    c == '_' || c == '-' || c == '.';
                if (!ok) chars[i] = '_';
            }
            return new string(chars);
        }

        private static DBDictionary GetOrCreateRootDict(Transaction tr, Database db)
        {
            var nod = (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead);
            if (!nod.Contains(RootKey))
            {
                nod.UpgradeOpen();
                var root = new DBDictionary();
                nod.SetAt(RootKey, root);
                tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(root, true);
                return root;
            }
            return (DBDictionary)tr.GetObject(nod.GetAt(RootKey), OpenMode.ForRead);
        }

        private static int ReadInt32OrDefault(ResultBuffer rb, int @default)
        {
            if (rb == null) return @default;
            foreach (TypedValue tv in rb)
                if (tv.TypeCode == DxfInt32 || tv.TypeCode == 90)
                    return Convert.ToInt32(tv.Value);
            return @default;
        }

        private static string Format(string prefix, int value, int width)
        {
            if (width < 1) width = 1;
            var num = value.ToString("D" + width);
            return string.IsNullOrEmpty(prefix) ? num : prefix + num;
        }
    }
}
```

```csharp
// File: PropertiesPalette.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.UI
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Windows;

namespace AutoCAD2020.UI

    public static class PropertiesPalette
    {
        private static PaletteSet _ps;
        private static CustomPropertiesUserControl _ui;

        public static void Show()
        {
            if (_ps == null)
            {
                _ps = new PaletteSet("CBI Properties", "CBI_Properties_Palette");
                _ui = new CustomPropertiesUserControl();
                _ps.Add("Properties", _ui);
            }
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        public static void OnCancelledOrIdle() => _ui?.OnCancelledOrIdle();
        public static void RefreshHome()       => _ui?.RefreshHomePreview();
    }
}
```

# 3) `CustomPropertiesUserControl.cs`  (your palette UI)

```csharp
// File: CustomPropertiesUserControl.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.UI
using System;
using System.Drawing;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;

namespace AutoCAD2020.UI
{
    public sealed class CustomPropertiesUserControl : UserControl
    {
        private readonly Button btnApply  = new Button { Text = "Apply"  };
        private readonly Button btnRevert = new Button { Text = "Revert" };
        private readonly Button btnSave   = new Button { Text = "Save"   };

        private readonly TextBox txtLayer      = new TextBox { Text = "C-ANNO-TAG" };
        private readonly TextBox txtTextHeight = new TextBox { Text = "0.125" };

        private readonly CheckBox chkAutoIncrement = new CheckBox { Text = "AutoIncrement", Checked = true };
        private readonly TextBox  txtPrefix        = new TextBox { Text = "PR-" };

        private readonly Label lblLineNext = new Label { AutoSize = true, Font = new Font("Segoe UI", 9F) };
        private readonly Label lblTagNext  = new Label { AutoSize = true, Font = new Font("Segoe UI", 9F) };

        public CustomPropertiesUserControl()
        {
            BuildLayout();
            WireEvents();
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        private void BuildLayout()
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
            Padding = new Padding(10);

            var top = new FlowLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, Height = 36 };
            top.Controls.AddRange(new Control[] { btnApply, btnRevert, btnSave });

            var grid = new TableLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, ColumnCount = 2, AutoSize = true };
            grid.Controls.Add(new Label { Text = "Layer", AutoSize = true }, 0, 0);
            grid.Controls.Add(txtLayer, 1, 0);
            grid.Controls.Add(new Label { Text = "TextHeight", AutoSize = true }, 0, 1);
            grid.Controls.Add(txtTextHeight, 1, 1);
            grid.Controls.Add(new Label { Text = "Prefix", AutoSize = true }, 0, 2);
            grid.Controls.Add(txtPrefix, 1, 2);
            grid.Controls.Add(chkAutoIncrement, 1, 3);

            var preview = new TableLayoutPanel { Dock = DockStyle.Top, ColumnCount = 1, AutoSize = true, Padding = new Padding(0,8,0,0) };
            preview.Controls.Add(lblLineNext, 0, 0);
            preview.Controls.Add(lblTagNext,  0, 1);

            var panel = new Panel { Dock = DockStyle.Fill, AutoScroll = true };
            panel.Controls.Add(preview);
            panel.Controls.Add(grid);

            Controls.Add(panel);
            Controls.Add(top);
        }

        private void WireEvents()
        {
            btnApply.Click  += (s, e) => OnApply();
            btnRevert.Click += (s, e) => OnRevert();
            btnSave.Click   += (s, e) => OnSave();

            txtPrefix.TextChanged += (s, e) => RefreshHomePreview();
            chkAutoIncrement.CheckedChanged += (s, e) => RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        private string Prefix => txtPrefix.Text ?? string.Empty;

        public void RefreshHomePreview()
        {
            lblLineNext.Text = "Line label next: " + NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", Prefix, 4);
            lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag label next:  " + NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG",  Prefix, 4);
        }

        public void OnCancelledOrIdle() => RefreshHomePreview();

        private void OnApply()
        {
            if (chkAutoIncrement.Checked)
            {
                var line = NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("LINE", Prefix, 4);
                var tag  = NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted("TAG",  Prefix, 4);
                var ed = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument?.Editor;
                ed?.WriteMessage($"\nApplied LINE: {line}, TAG: {tag}");
            }
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        private void OnRevert()
        {
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }

        private void OnSave()
        {
            // TODO: persist settings (layer, textheight, prefix) to your store.
            var ed = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument?.Editor;
            ed?.WriteMessage("\nCBI Properties: settings saved.");
            RefreshHomePreview();
        }
    }
}
```

# 4) (If missing) Hook ESC/End to refresh

Wherever you initialize your plugin (your `IExtensionApplication.Initialize()`), wire:

```csharp
// Example in your plugin init:
var mgr = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager;
foreach (var d in mgr) { HookDoc(d as Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Document); }
mgr.DocumentCreated += (s,e) => HookDoc(e.Document);

void HookDoc(Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Document doc)
{
    if (doc == null) return;
    doc.CommandCancelled += (s, e) => AutoCAD2020.UI.PropertiesPalette.OnCancelledOrIdle();
    doc.CommandEnded     += (s, e) => AutoCAD2020.UI.PropertiesPalette.OnCancelledOrIdle();
}
```

// File: PluginEntry.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020
// Purpose: Initialize palette and wire global command-end/cancel callbacks.

using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;
using AutoCAD2020.UI;

[assembly: CommandClass(typeof(AutoCAD2020.PluginEntry))]

namespace AutoCAD2020
{
    public class PluginEntry : IExtensionApplication
    {
        public void Initialize()
        {
            // Hook existing documents and new ones to refresh palette on cancel/end
            var mgr = Application.DocumentManager;
            foreach (Document d in mgr) HookDoc(d);
            mgr.DocumentCreated += (s, e) => HookDoc(e.Document);
        }

        private static void HookDoc(Document doc)
        {
            doc.CommandCancelled += (s, e) => PropertiesPalette.OnCancelledOrIdle();
            doc.CommandEnded += (s, e) => PropertiesPalette.OnCancelledOrIdle();
        }

        public void Terminate() { }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROPERTIES")]
        public void CmdShowPropertiesPalette()
        {
            PropertiesPalette.Show();
        }
    }
}

## Response:
10/6/2025, 4:42:59 PM

> **Outlining Properties Hub architecture**
>
> The user wants guidance on the properties hub’s design. It helps to outline how the system's orchestrator routes to providers based on selection. The palette handles source, selection, apply, revert, and save functions, while the property grid organizes sections like Appearance, Behavior, and General. The system uses providers for components, PipeRuns, and Instruments, with PropertyRouter deciding the active provider. Other components, like LineTagSettings and LayerRules, enforce correct settings and behavior.
>
> Thought for 8s

Ahh—this makes sense now. You already have a **Properties Hub** layer, and we accidentally started rebuilding a second palette beside it. Let’s realign with your existing hub.

Here’s what your **Properties Hub** looks like (based on the files in your screenshot) and what each piece is supposed to do, plus exactly what to change to add the “home preview” (next Line/Tag numbers after ESC/cancel).

---

# What each file is for (the intended architecture)

**Palette host**
- **`CbiPropertiesPalette.cs`**  
  The real palette UI for “CBI Properties.” Hosts `PropertiesControl` and the top bar (Source/Selection | Apply | Revert | Save). It should *not* own business logic; it delegates to the hub/router.

**View + orchestration**
- **`PropertiesControl.cs`**  
  The WinForms/WPF user control that shows the property grid/sections (Appearance, Behavior, General). Binds to a model coming from a provider (below).
- **`PropertyRouter.cs`**  
  Inspects the current selection and decides **which provider** is in charge (pipe run, component, instrument, generic tag). Exposes `GetProvider(ObjectId)` and/or `GetActiveModel()`.

**Providers + models**
- **`PipeRunPropertyProvider.cs` / `PipeRunProperties.cs`**  
  Specialized provider and model (properties like Layer, TextHeight, Slope?, etc.) for pipe runs; knows how to **Apply**, **Revert**, **Save** for that type.
- **`ComponentPropertyProvider.cs` / `ComponentProperties.cs`**  
  Same pattern for general components (valves, fittings).
- **`InstrumentPropertyProvider.cs` / `InstrumentProperties.cs`**  
  Same for instruments.
- **`LineTagSettings.cs`**  
  Shared settings for line tags: `Prefix`, `AutoIncrement`, `TextHeight`, etc. Used by providers and palette.

**Rules + helpers**
- **`LayerRules.cs` / `LayerNameConverter.cs`**  
  Enforce/convert layer names from your standards.
- **`XDataHelpers.cs`**  
  Read/write XData/XRecord for your objects.
- **`PipeRunMatchService.cs` / `PipeRunMatchCommands.cs`**  
  “Find the pipe run” logic, recognition/selection helpers.

**Other**
- **`TagNumberingService.cs`** (under Services)  
  A thin wrapper that (now) should call **`NodLineNumberStore`** for counters.

---

# What we were doing (and what broke)

- You asked that **after ESC/cancel** the palette **doesn’t clear**; it should show a **home state** with:
  - **Line Label next:** (preview)
  - **Tag Label next:** (preview)
- We added `Peek()`/`NextFormatted()` into **`NodLineNumberStore`** to support those previews.
- Then we accidentally built a second palette (`CustomPropertiesUserControl` / `PropertiesPalette`) which collided with your existing **Properties Hub**.

Let’s undo the collision and add the features to your **existing hub**.

---

# Minimal, safe integration plan (keep your hub; add the previews)

## 1) Keep the finalized `NodLineNumberStore` (the one you posted last)
No changes needed there.

## 2) Update **`CbiPropertiesPalette.cs`** (the real palette)
Add two labels (or reuse a status area) and a couple of methods.

```csharp
// inside CbiPropertiesPalette.cs
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services; // NodLineNumberStore

// add fields
private Label _lblLineNext;
private Label _lblTagNext;

private string CurrentPrefix => _view?.Model?.LineTagSettings?.Prefix ?? "PR-";

// call this in the palette constructor after InitializeComponent()
private void BuildHomePreviewArea()
{
    _lblLineNext = new Label { AutoSize = true, Text = "" };
    _lblTagNext  = new Label { AutoSize = true, Text = "" };

    // place these under the toolbar, or at top of PropertiesControl
    // e.g., somePanel.Controls.Add(_lblLineNext);
    //       somePanel.Controls.Add(_lblTagNext);
}

// public API called by PluginEntry on cancel/end
public void OnCancelledOrIdle()
{
    RefreshHomePreview();
}

// show non-incrementing previews
public void RefreshHomePreview()
{
    var prefix = CurrentPrefix;
    _lblLineNext.Text = "Line label next: " + NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", prefix, 4);
    _lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag label next:  " + NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG",  prefix, 4);
}
```

Also wire your **Apply/Revert/Save** buttons to call a shared method:

```csharp
private void OnApplyClick(object sender, EventArgs e)
{
    var provider = _router?.GetActiveProvider();
    provider?.Apply(_view?.Model);   // your existing provider pattern
    RefreshHomePreview();            // update the “next” immediately
}

private void OnRevertClick(object sender, EventArgs e)
{
    var provider = _router?.GetActiveProvider();
    provider?.Revert(_view?.Model);
    RefreshHomePreview();
}

private void OnSaveClick(object sender, EventArgs e)
{
    var provider = _router?.GetActiveProvider();
    provider?.Save(_view?.Model);
    RefreshHomePreview();
}
```

If your palette lets users edit **Prefix** in `LineTagSettings` live, hook its change to `RefreshHomePreview()` as well.

```csharp
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Windows;

namespace AutoCAD2020.UI
{
    public static class PropertiesPalette

            _ui.RefreshHomePreview(); // show previews on open
        }

        public static void OnCancelledOrIdle() => _ui?.OnCancelledOrIdle();
        public static void RefreshHome()       => _ui?.RefreshHomePreview();
    }
}
```

# Where the **Home Preview** pulls values from

- **Prefix** → from your hub model (`LineTagSettings.Prefix`)  
  - If that model isn’t initialized yet, fall back to `"PR-"`.
- **Next numbers** → `NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", prefix, 4)` and `Peek("TAG", prefix, 4)`  
  - Non-incrementing.
- **On Apply** (when you actually place/confirm labels), your provider should call `NodLineNumberStore.NextFormatted(...)` where appropriate.

---

# Sanity checklist

- [ ] `PropertiesPalette` hosts **`CbiPropertiesPalette`** (not the old one).
- [ ] `CbiPropertiesPalette` has `RefreshHomePreview()` and `OnCancelledOrIdle()`.
- [ ] `PluginEntry` calls `PropertiesPalette.OnCancelledOrIdle()` on `CommandCancelled` and `CommandEnded`.
- [ ] Only **one** `NodLineNumberStore.cs` in the solution.

// v0.2.1 — CBI Properties Palette host (C# 7.3)
// - Named handlers for reliable unsubscribe
// - Clears palette on ESC / no selection via _ui.Clear()
// - Per-document attach/detach for selection + command lifecycle
// - Float/Dock helpers + test commands
// - Size helpers used by PropertiesControl's resize grip

using System;
using System.Drawing;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Windows;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public static class CbiPropertiesPalette
    {
        private const string PaletteTitle = "CBI Properties";
        private static readonly Size InitialSize = new Size(520, 600);
        private static readonly Size MinSize = new Size(300, 220);

        private static PaletteSet _ps;
        private static PropertiesControl _ui;
        private static bool _hooked;
        private static SelectionContext _lastCtx;

        // ---------- Public entry point ----------
        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_PALETTE")]
        public static void CmdShow()
        {
            Show();
            RefreshFromSelection();
        }

        public static void Show()
        {
            if (_ps == null)
            {
                _ui = new PropertiesControl();
                _ui.ApplyRequested += delegate { PropertyRouter.ApplyIfPossible(_ui.SelectedModel, _lastCtx); };

                _ps = new PaletteSet(PaletteTitle)
                {
                    DockEnabled = DockSides.Left | DockSides.Right | DockSides.None,
                    MinimumSize = MinSize,
                    Size = InitialSize,
                    Style = PaletteSetStyles.ShowCloseButton |
                                  PaletteSetStyles.ShowAutoHideButton |
                                  PaletteSetStyles.Snappable
                };

                _ps.Add("Properties", _ui);
            }

            _ps.Visible = true;

            if (!_hooked)
            {
                // Attach for current doc (if any)
                var dm = Application.DocumentManager;
                if (dm.MdiActiveDocument != null)
                    AttachHandlersTo(dm.MdiActiveDocument);

                // Rewire when document changes
                dm.DocumentActivated += OnDocumentActivated;

                _hooked = true;
            }
        }

        // ---------- Selection & command wiring ----------
        private static void OnDocumentActivated(object sender, DocumentCollectionEventArgs e)
        {
            var dm = Application.DocumentManager;

            // Detach from all open docs to be safe (cheap)
            foreach (Document d in dm)
                DetachHandlersFrom(d);

            // Attach to the newly active doc
            if (e.Document != null)
                AttachHandlersTo(e.Document);

            // Re-evaluate current selection
            RefreshFromSelection();
        }

        private static void AttachHandlersTo(Document d)
        {
            if (d == null) return;

            // Selection events
            d.Editor.SelectionAdded += OnSelectionAdded;
            d.Editor.SelectionRemoved += OnSelectionRemoved;

            // Command lifecycle (ESC etc.)
            d.CommandEnded += OnCommandEnded;
            d.CommandCancelled += OnCommandCancelled;
            d.CommandFailed += OnCommandFailed;
        }

        private static void DetachHandlersFrom(Document d)
        {
            if (d == null) return;

            // Selection events
            d.Editor.SelectionAdded -= OnSelectionAdded;
            d.Editor.SelectionRemoved -= OnSelectionRemoved;

            // Command lifecycle
            d.CommandEnded -= OnCommandEnded;
            d.CommandCancelled -= OnCommandCancelled;
            d.CommandFailed -= OnCommandFailed;
        }

        private static void ClearSelectionAndUI()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

            var ed = doc.Editor;

            try
            {
                // Force-clear the PICKFIRST/implied selection
                ed.SetImpliedSelection(new Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices.ObjectId[0]);
            }
            catch { /* ignore */ }

            _lastCtx = null;
            _ui.Clear();      // hard blank the palette
        }

        private static void OnSelectionAdded(object sender, SelectionAddedEventArgs e) => RefreshFromSelection();
        private static void OnSelectionRemoved(object sender, SelectionRemovedEventArgs e) => RefreshFromSelection();
        private static void OnCommandEnded(object sender, CommandEventArgs e) => ClearSelectionAndUI();
        private static void OnCommandCancelled(object sender, CommandEventArgs e) => ClearSelectionAndUI();
        private static void OnCommandFailed(object sender, CommandEventArgs e) => ClearSelectionAndUI();

        // ---------- Core refresh logic ----------
        private static void RefreshFromSelection()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

            var ed = doc.Editor;
            var implied = ed.SelectImplied();

            // Nothing selected → hard clear
            if (implied.Status != PromptStatus.OK || implied.Value == null || implied.Value.Count == 0)
            {
                _lastCtx = null;
                _ui.Clear();               // << blank panel (requires Clear() in PropertiesControl)
                return;
            }

            // Use first picked object (expand to multi-select later)
            var id = implied.Value[0].ObjectId;
            _lastCtx = new SelectionContext(id, doc);

            var model = PropertyRouter.Resolve(_lastCtx);
            if (model != null)
                _ui.Bind(model, "Selection");
            else
                _ui.Clear();               // unclaimed selection → blank
        }

        // ---------- Size & docking helpers (used by resize grip and test cmds) ----------
        public static Size GetSize()
        {
            return _ps != null ? _ps.Size : InitialSize;
        }

        public static void EnsureFloating()
        {
            if (_ps == null) return;
            if (_ps.Dock != DockSides.None)
            {
                if (_ps.Location.IsEmpty || _ps.Location.X <= 0 || _ps.Location.Y <= 0)
                    _ps.Location = new Point(120, 120);
                _ps.Dock = DockSides.None;
            }
        }

        public static void SetSize(Size size)
        {
            if (_ps == null) return;
            if (_ps.Dock != DockSides.None) EnsureFloating();

            if (size.Width < MinSize.Width) size.Width = MinSize.Width;
            if (size.Height < MinSize.Height) size.Height = MinSize.Height;

            _ps.Size = size;
        }

        // Convenience: quickly float/dock from the command line for testing
        public static void FloatAndResize(Size size)
        {
            Show();
            EnsureFloating();
            SetSize(size);
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        public static void DockLeft()
        {
            Show();
            _ps.Dock = DockSides.Left;
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        public static void DockRight()
        {
            Show();
            _ps.Dock = DockSides.Right;
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_FLOAT")]
        public static void CmdFloat() => FloatAndResize(InitialSize);

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_DOCKLEFT")]
        public static void CmdDockLeft() => DockLeft();

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_DOCKRIGHT")]
        public static void CmdDockRight() => DockRight();
    }
}

// v0.1.1 (C# 7.3) — Provider registry + resolution (no records)

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public class SelectionContext
    {
        public ObjectId Id { get; private set; }
        public Document Doc { get; private set; }
        public SelectionContext(ObjectId id, Document doc) { Id = id; Doc = doc; }
    }

    public interface IPropertySourceProvider
    {
        bool CanProvideFor(SelectionContext ctx);
        object GetSelectedObject(SelectionContext ctx);
        void Apply(object editedModel, SelectionContext ctx);
    }

    public static class PropertyRouter
    {
        // KEEP ONLY THIS ONE
        private static readonly List<IPropertySourceProvider> _providers = new List<IPropertySourceProvider>
        {
            new PipeRunPropertyProvider(),
            new InstrumentPropertyProvider(),
            new ComponentPropertyProvider(),
            new LineTagSettingsProvider()
        };

        public static object Resolve(SelectionContext ctx)
        {
            foreach (var p in _providers)
            {
                try { if (p.CanProvideFor(ctx)) return p.GetSelectedObject(ctx); }
                catch { }
            }
            return ResolveForTool();
        }

        public static object ResolveForTool() { return MasterProperties.LineTag; }

        public static void ApplyIfPossible(object model, SelectionContext ctx)
        {
            if (model == null) return;

            if (ctx != null)
            {
                foreach (var p in _providers)
                {
                    try
                    {
                        if (p.CanProvideFor(ctx))
                        {
                            var current = p.GetSelectedObject(ctx);
                            if (current != null && current.GetType() == model.GetType())
                            {
                                p.Apply(model, ctx);
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    catch { }
                }
            }

            if (object.ReferenceEquals(model, MasterProperties.LineTag))
                MasterProperties.Save();
        }
    }
}

// v0.1.1 (C# 7.3) — PropertyGrid UI; switched to Newtonsoft.Json

using System;
using System.ComponentModel;
using System.IO;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using System.Drawing;              // <-- needed for Point/Size/Color/Cursors
using Newtonsoft.Json;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public partial class PropertiesControl : UserControl
    {
        private readonly PropertyGrid _grid = new PropertyGrid();
        private readonly ToolStrip _bar = new ToolStrip();
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lbl = new ToolStripLabel("Source:");
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblSource = new ToolStripLabel("—");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnApply = new ToolStripButton("Apply");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnRevert = new ToolStripButton("Revert");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnSave = new ToolStripButton("Save");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnLoad = new ToolStripButton("Load");
        private readonly ToolStripSeparator _sep = new ToolStripSeparator();
        private readonly ToolStripControlHost _chkAutoHost;
        private readonly CheckBox _chkAuto = new CheckBox { Text = "Auto-apply", Checked = true };

        private object _currentModel;
        private object _snapshot;

        // --- resize grip state ---
        private readonly Panel _grip = new Panel();
        private bool _dragging;
        private Point _dragStartScreen;
        private Size _startSize;

        public event EventHandler ApplyRequested;
        public object SelectedModel { get { return _currentModel; } }

        public PropertiesControl()
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill;

            _grid.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
            _grid.PropertyValueChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                if (_chkAuto.Checked && ApplyRequested != null) ApplyRequested(this, EventArgs.Empty);
            };

            _chkAutoHost = new ToolStripControlHost(_chkAuto) { Margin = new Padding(8, 2, 4, 2) };
            _btnApply.Click += (s, e) => { if (ApplyRequested != null) ApplyRequested(this, EventArgs.Empty); };
            _btnRevert.Click += (s, e) => Rebind(_snapshot);
            _btnSave.Click += (s, e) => SavePreset();
            _btnLoad.Click += (s, e) => LoadPreset();

            _bar.Items.Add(_lbl);
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblSource);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnApply);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnRevert);
            _bar.Items.Add(_sep);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnSave);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnLoad);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
            _bar.Items.Add(_chkAutoHost);
            _bar.Dock = DockStyle.Top;

            Controls.Add(_grid);
            Controls.Add(_bar);

            // --- resize grip setup (bottom-right corner) ---
            _grip.Size = new Size(14, 14);
            _grip.Anchor = AnchorStyles.Bottom | AnchorStyles.Right;
            _grip.Cursor = Cursors.SizeNWSE;
            _grip.BackColor = Color.Transparent; // invisible; cursor indicates grip
            _grip.Location = new Point(Width - _grip.Width - 2, Height - _grip.Height - 2);

            _grip.MouseDown += (s, e) =>
            {
                //if (e.Button != MouseButtons.Left) return;
                //_dragging = true;
                //_dragStartScreen = Cursor.Position;
                //_startSize = CbiPropertiesPalette.GetSize(); // palette current size
                //_grip.Capture = true;

if (e.Button != MouseButtons.Left) return;
                CbiPropertiesPalette.EnsureFloating();  // <-- make sure we’re floating
                _dragging = true;
                _dragStartScreen = Cursor.Position;
                _startSize = CbiPropertiesPalette.GetSize();
                _grip.Capture = true;

            };
            _grip.MouseMove += (s, e) =>
            {
                if (!_dragging) return;
                var cur = Cursor.Position;
                int dx = cur.X - _dragStartScreen.X;
                int dy = cur.Y - _dragStartScreen.Y;
                var newSize = new Size(_startSize.Width + dx, _startSize.Height + dy);
                CbiPropertiesPalette.SetSize(newSize);       // enforce min size inside host
            };
            _grip.MouseUp += (s, e) =>
            {
                _dragging = false;
                _grip.Capture = false;
            };

            this.Resize += (s, e) =>
            {
                _grip.Location = new Point(Width - _grip.Width - 2, Height - _grip.Height - 2);
            };

            _grid.PropertyValueChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                _grid.Refresh();

                var propName = e.ChangedItem?.PropertyDescriptor?.Name;
                bool forceApply =
                    string.Equals(propName, nameof(PipeRunProperties.LayerName), System.StringComparison.Ordinal) ||
                    string.Equals(propName, nameof(PipeRunProperties.PipingRunType), System.StringComparison.Ordinal);

                if (_chkAuto.Checked || forceApply)
                    ApplyRequested?.Invoke(this, System.EventArgs.Empty);
            };

            Controls.Add(_grip);
        }

        public void Clear()
        {
            _currentModel = null;
            _snapshot = null;
            _grid.SelectedObject = null;
            _lblSource.Text = "—";   // resets the header
        }

        public void Bind(object model, string sourceLabel)
        {
            if (model == null) model = new Placeholder();
            _currentModel = model;
            _snapshot = DeepClone(model);
            _grid.SelectedObject = _currentModel;
            _lblSource.Text = string.IsNullOrEmpty(sourceLabel) ? InferLabel(model) : sourceLabel;
        }

        private void Rebind(object snap)
        {
            _currentModel = DeepClone(snap ?? new Placeholder());
            _grid.SelectedObject = _currentModel;
        }

        private static object DeepClone(object instance)
        {
            if (instance == null) return null;
            var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(instance);
            return JsonConvert.DeserializeObject(json, instance.GetType());
        }

        private string InferLabel(object model)
        {
            return model == null ? "—" : model.GetType().Name;
        }

        private void SavePreset()
        {
            if (_currentModel == null) return;
            using (var sfd = new SaveFileDialog
            {
                Filter = "JSON (*.json)|*.json",
                FileName = _currentModel.GetType().Name + ".json"
            })
            {
                if (sfd.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK) return;
                var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(_currentModel, Formatting.Indented);
                File.WriteAllText(sfd.FileName, json);
            }
        }

        private void LoadPreset()
        {
            if (_currentModel == null) return;
            using (var ofd = new OpenFileDialog { Filter = "JSON (*.json)|*.json" })
            {
                if (ofd.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK) return;
                var json = File.ReadAllText(ofd.FileName);
                var loaded = JsonConvert.DeserializeObject(json, _currentModel.GetType());
                if (loaded != null) Bind(loaded, _lblSource.Text);
            }
        }

        private sealed class Placeholder
        {
            [Category("Info")]
            [DisplayName("Tip")]
            public string Message
            {
                get { return "Select an entity or run a tool to see its properties here."; }
            }
        }
    }
}

// v0.1.1 (C# 7.3) — Tool settings + Newtonsoft persistence

using System.ComponentModel;
using System.IO;
using Newtonsoft.Json;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public class LineTagSettings
    {
        [Category("Appearance")]
        [Description("Height of annotation text in drawing units.")]
        public double TextHeight { get; set; } = 0.125;

        [Category("Appearance")]
        [Description("Layer to place tag entities on.")]
        public string Layer { get; set; } = "C-ANNO-TAG";

        [Category("General")]
        [Description("String prepended to the computed tag.")]
        public string Prefix { get; set; } = "PR-";

        [Category("Behavior")]
        [Description("If true, increments a counter on each placement.")]
        public bool AutoIncrement { get; set; } = true;
    }

    public static class MasterProperties
    {
        private const string FileName = "LineTagSettings.json";
        private static LineTagSettings _lineTag;
        public static LineTagSettings LineTag
        {
            get { return _lineTag ?? (_lineTag = Load() ?? new LineTagSettings()); }
        }

        public static void Save()
        {
            var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(LineTag, Formatting.Indented);
            File.WriteAllText(FileName, json);
        }

        private static LineTagSettings Load()
        {
            if (!File.Exists(FileName)) return null;
            var json = File.ReadAllText(FileName);
            return JsonConvert.DeserializeObject<LineTagSettings>(json);
        }
    }

    public sealed class LineTagSettingsProvider : IPropertySourceProvider
    {
        public bool CanProvideFor(SelectionContext ctx) { return false; } // tool-only
        public object GetSelectedObject(SelectionContext ctx) { return null; }
        public void Apply(object editedModel, SelectionContext ctx) { }
    }
}

using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Services
{
    public static class TagNumberingService
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Assigns next IDs to selected valves, updates INDEX, mirrors to linked bubbles.
        /// Example format: "V-####" (pad 4, global scope).
        /// </summary>
        public static void AutoNumberSelection(string prefix = "V", int pad = 4, string scope = "GLOBAL")
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            var db = doc.Database;
            var ed = doc.Editor;

            var filter = new SelectionFilter(new[] { new TypedValue((int)DxfCode.Start, "INSERT") });
            var psr = ed.GetSelection(new PromptSelectionOptions { MessageForAdding = "\nSelect valves to auto-number: " }, filter);
            if (psr.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            int changed = 0, skipped = 0;

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                foreach (SelectedObject so in psr.Value)
                {
                    var br = tr.GetObject(so.ObjectId, OpenMode.ForRead) as BlockReference;
                    if (br == null) continue;

                    // Allocate next number and format the ID
                    int next = Block_Operations.TagIndexUtil.AllocateNext(tr, scope);
                    var newId = Block_Operations.TagIndexUtil.FormatId(prefix, next, pad);

                    // Check duplicates just in case (should be unique by allocation)
                    var existingHandle = Block_Operations.TagIndexUtil.FindHandleById(tr, newId);
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(existingHandle))
                    {
                        skipped++;
                        continue;
                    }

                    // Write attribute
                    if (!Block_Operations.ValveBubbleLinkUtil.SetAttributeSafe(br, tr, Block_Operations.ValveBubbleLinkUtil.ValveIdTag, newId))
                    {
                        skipped++;
                        continue;
                    }

                    // Register in index
                    Block_Operations.TagIndexUtil.TryRegisterId(tr, newId, br.Handle.ToString(), out _);

                    // Sync children (if any)
                    Block_Operations.ValveBubbleLinkUtil.SyncChildrenFromParent(br, tr);

                    changed++;
                }
                tr.Commit();
            }

            ed.WriteMessage($"\nAuto-numbered {changed} valve(s). Skipped {skipped}.");
        }
    }
}

using AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using static AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub.PipeRunProperties;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public sealed class PipeRunPropertyProvider : IPropertySourceProvider
    {
        private const string AppName = "CBI_PIPE_RUN";

        public bool CanProvideFor(SelectionContext ctx)
        {
            // If already stamped, definitely ours
            if (XDataHelpers.HasAppName(ctx.Id, AppName)) return true;

            // Otherwise, claim common pipe geometry so first Apply can stamp XData
            using (var tr = ctx.Doc.TransactionManager.StartOpenCloseTransaction())
            {
                var ent = tr.GetObject(ctx.Id, OpenMode.ForRead) as Entity;
                if (ent == null) return false;

                return ent is Polyline || ent is Polyline2d || ent is Polyline3d;
            }
        }

        public object GetSelectedObject(SelectionContext ctx)
        {
            var map = XDataHelpers.Read(ctx.Id, AppName);
            var p = new PipeRunProperties();

            // Layer (prefer XData, else actual entity layer)
            using (var tr = ctx.Doc.TransactionManager.StartOpenCloseTransaction())
            {
                var ent = (Entity)tr.GetObject(ctx.Id, OpenMode.ForRead);
                p.LayerName = map.Get("LayerName") ?? ent.Layer;
            }

            // Identification
            p.FluidCode = map.Get("FluidCode");
            p.FluidSystem = map.Get("FluidSystem");
            p.PlantGroupName = map.Get("PlantGroupName");
            p.PlantGroupType = map.Get("PlantGroupType");
            p.PlantItemType = map.Get("PlantItemType");
            p.TagSeqNo = map.Get("TagSeqNo");
            p.TagSuffix = map.Get("TagSuffix");
            p.UnitNumber = map.Get("UnitNumber");

            // Piping Run Type (string → enum)
            var prt = map.Get("PipingRunType");
            PipeRunKind kindVal;
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(prt))
            {
                if (System.Enum.TryParse(prt, true, out kindVal))
                    p.PipingRunType = kindVal;
                else
                    p.PipingRunType = null; // unknown/legacy
            }

            // Physical
            p.InsulationPurpose = map.Get("InsulationPurpose");
            p.NominalDiameter = map.Get("NominalDiameter");
            p.PipingMaterialClass = map.Get("PipingMaterialClass");

            return p;
        }

        public void Apply(object editedModel, SelectionContext ctx)
        {
            var m = (PipeRunProperties)editedModel;

            var itemTag = PipeRunProperties.BuildItemTag(
                m.NominalDiameter, m.FluidCode, m.TagSeqNo, m.PipingMaterialClass, m.InsulationPurpose);

            EnsureRegApp(ctx.Doc.Database, AppName);

            var map = new XDataMap
            {
                ["SchemaVersion"] = "1.0",
                ["LayerName"] = m.LayerName,
                ["FluidCode"] = m.FluidCode,
                ["FluidSystem"] = m.FluidSystem,
                ["PlantGroupName"] = m.PlantGroupName,
                ["PlantGroupType"] = m.PlantGroupType,
                ["PlantItemType"] = m.PlantItemType,
                ["TagSeqNo"] = m.TagSeqNo,
                ["TagSuffix"] = m.TagSuffix,
                ["UnitNumber"] = m.UnitNumber,

                // write enum as string ("Primary" / "Secondary")
                ["PipingRunType"] = m.PipingRunType?.ToString(),

                ["InsulationPurpose"] = m.InsulationPurpose,
                ["NominalDiameter"] = m.NominalDiameter,
                ["PipingMaterialClass"] = m.PipingMaterialClass,
                ["ItemTag"] = itemTag
            };
            XDataHelpers.Write(ctx.Id, AppName, map);

            // Decide target layer: user-specified wins; else CAD standard from enum
            var targetLayer = !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(m.LayerName)
                                ? m.LayerName
                                : LayerRules.LayerForPipeRun(m.PipingRunType);

            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(targetLayer))
            {
                EnsureLayerExists(ctx.Doc.Database, targetLayer);
                using (var tr = ctx.Doc.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
                {
                    var ent = (Entity)tr.GetObject(ctx.Id, OpenMode.ForWrite);
                    if (ent != null && !ent.IsErased) ent.Layer = targetLayer;
                    tr.Commit();
                }
            }
        }

        // helper (drop at bottom of file or into XDataHelpers if you prefer)
        private static void EnsureRegApp(Database db, string appName)
        {
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var rat = (RegAppTable)tr.GetObject(db.RegAppTableId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!rat.Has(appName))
                {
                    rat.UpgradeOpen();
                    var rec = new RegAppTableRecord { Name = appName };
                    rat.Add(rec);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(rec, true);
                }
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

        private static void EnsureLayerExists(Database db, string layerName)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(layerName)) return;

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var lt = (LayerTable)tr.GetObject(db.LayerTableId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!lt.Has(layerName))
                {
                    lt.UpgradeOpen();
                    var rec = new LayerTableRecord { Name = layerName };
                    lt.Add(rec);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(rec, true);
                }
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

}
}

You’re right—we should wire the **home preview** into your existing **Properties Hub** (not a new palette). I reviewed the code you pasted, and here’s exactly what to change—surgically—so that after ESC/cancel or when nothing is selected, the palette shows:

- **Line label next:** (peek, non-incrementing)  
- **Tag label next:** (peek, non-incrementing)

…and when Apply/Revert/Save is clicked, the preview refreshes.

Below are **minimal diffs** to three files:

---

# 1) `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs` — use “Home” instead of clearing

### What changes
- Replace calls to `_ui.Clear()` on cancel/end/no selection with `_ui.ShowHome(prefix)` (non-blank).
- Keep selection-binding behavior when something *is* selected.

### Patch
```csharp
// add near the top
using AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub;         // already there
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;       // for NodLineNumberStore (used by UI)
...
// helper to get current prefix from your master settings
private static string CurrentPrefix()
{
    try { return MasterProperties.LineTag?.Prefix ?? "PR-"; }
    catch { return "PR-"; }
}
...
private static void ClearSelectionAndUI()
{
    var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
    if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

    try
    {
        doc.Editor.SetImpliedSelection(new Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices.ObjectId[0]);
    }
    catch { /* ignore */ }

    _lastCtx = null;
    _ui.ShowHome(CurrentPrefix());   // << instead of _ui.Clear();
}
...
private static void RefreshFromSelection()
{
    var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
    if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

    var ed = doc.Editor;
    var implied = ed.SelectImplied();

    if (implied.Status != PromptStatus.OK || implied.Value == null || implied.Value.Count == 0)
    {
        _lastCtx = null;
        _ui.ShowHome(CurrentPrefix());   // << instead of _ui.Clear();
        return;
    }

    var id = implied.Value[0].ObjectId;
    _lastCtx = new SelectionContext(id, doc);

    var model = PropertyRouter.Resolve(_lastCtx);
    if (model != null)
        _ui.Bind(model, "Selection");
    else
        _ui.ShowHome(CurrentPrefix());   // << unclaimed → Home, not blank
}
```

---

# 2) `PropertiesControl.cs` — add two preview labels + API

### What changes
- Add two small labels in the toolbar (or you can put them below it—this keeps it simple).
- Add public methods:
  - `ShowHome(string prefix)`
  - `RefreshHomePreview(string prefix)` (can also be called after Apply/Revert/Save)

### Patch
```csharp
// add at top of file
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;   // NodLineNumberStore
...
public partial class PropertiesControl : UserControl
{
    ...
    // add toolbar preview labels
    private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblLineNext = new ToolStripLabel();
    private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblTagNext  = new ToolStripLabel();
    ...
    public PropertiesControl()
    {
        ...
        _lblLineNext.Alignment = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right;
        _lblTagNext.Alignment  = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right;

        // order: [Source] ... [Apply][Revert]|[Save][Load] ... [Auto-apply] ... [previews]
        _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
        _bar.Items.Add(_lblTagNext);
        _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("  "));
        _bar.Items.Add(_lblLineNext);
        _bar.Dock = DockStyle.Top;
        ...
    }
    ...
    // ---- NEW: show "Home" (no selection) with previews ----
    public void ShowHome(string prefix)
    {
        // keep the existing placeholder model, but refresh previews
        Bind(new Placeholder(), "Source: Tool");
        RefreshHomePreview(prefix);
    }

    // ---- NEW: recompute non-incrementing previews ----
    public void RefreshHomePreview(string prefix)
    {
        try
        {
            var p = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(prefix) ? "PR-" : prefix;
            var line = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", p, 4); // no increment
            var tag  = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG",  p, 4); // no increment
            _lblLineNext.Text = $"Line next: {line}";
            _lblTagNext.Text  = $"Tag next: {tag}";
        }
        catch
        {
            _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
            _lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag next: —";
        }
    }
}
```

> Note: `Clear()` remains for rare “hard blank” needs, but the palette will normally call `ShowHome(prefix)`.

---

# 3) Hook Apply/Revert/Save to refresh the preview

You already raise `ApplyRequested` and handle Rebind/Save. Just add a **single** refresh line after each action. Since `PropertiesControl` doesn’t know the current prefix source, we’ll have **`CbiPropertiesPalette`** call `RefreshHomePreview(CurrentPrefix())` when buttons fire.

### Patch in `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs` (where you wire Apply button)
You already have:
```csharp
_ui = new PropertiesControl();
_ui.ApplyRequested += delegate { PropertyRouter.ApplyIfPossible(_ui.SelectedModel, _lastCtx); };
```
Change to:
```csharp
_ui = new PropertiesControl();
_ui.ApplyRequested += delegate
{
    PropertyRouter.ApplyIfPossible(_ui.SelectedModel, _lastCtx);
    _ui.RefreshHomePreview(CurrentPrefix());   // << keep preview correct after apply
};
```

### Patch for Revert/Save (two options)
If you want the palette host to refresh after those too, wire their clicks in `PropertiesControl` to raise a tiny event (or simplest: let the palette refresh when commands end/cancel—which you already do). If you prefer surgical:

Add a tiny event in `PropertiesControl`:
```csharp
public event EventHandler AnyActionCompleted; // raise after Apply/Revert/Save
```
Raise it in the three handlers (`Apply`, `Revert`, `Save`), then in `CbiPropertiesPalette.Show()`:
```csharp
_ui.AnyActionCompleted += (s,e) => _ui.RefreshHomePreview(CurrentPrefix());
```

But honestly, since `Apply` is already covered and you call `ShowHome` on command boundaries, you can skip this unless you need instant preview after `Revert/Save`.

---

## That’s it

### Behavior after these changes
- No selection / ESC / command end → palette shows **Home** with **next Line/Tag** previews based on `MasterProperties.LineTag.Prefix`.
- Selecting an entity → palette shows its bound model (as before).
- Clicking **Apply** → your provider runs; palette then refreshes the preview labels immediately.
- You didn’t have to replace your architecture—just enabled the home state.

And if your prefix can change live in the grid (`LineTagSettings.Prefix`), tell me where it’s edited—I’ll add a one-liner to call `RefreshHomePreview(CurrentPrefix())` on that property’s change (you already have a `PropertyValueChanged` handler we can piggyback).
