> Thought for 17s

Totally—here’s a **drop-in replacement** for your existing `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs` that keeps your wiring, but instead of blanking the UI it **falls back to the tool settings** (`MasterProperties.LineTag`) whenever there’s no valid selection (after ESC/cancel, end of command, or empty PICKFIRST).

It does **not** require any changes to `PropertiesControl` (still uses `Bind(...)` and `Clear()` only), so it should compile against what you already have.

```csharp
// v0.2.2 — CBI Properties Palette host (C# 7.3)
// Change: when there is no selection (or on ESC/end), bind the LineTag tool
//         settings instead of clearing the UI. This gives a stable "Home" view.
//         No changes required to PropertiesControl.

using System;
using System.Drawing;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Windows;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public static class CbiPropertiesPalette
    {
        private const string PaletteTitle = "CBI Properties";
        private static readonly Size InitialSize = new Size(520, 600);
        private static readonly Size MinSize     = new Size(300, 220);

        private static PaletteSet _ps;
        private static PropertiesControl _ui;
        private static bool _hooked;
        private static SelectionContext _lastCtx;

        // ---------- Public entry point ----------
        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_PALETTE")]
        public static void CmdShow()
        {
            Show();
            RefreshFromSelection();
        }

        public static void Show()
        {
            if (_ps == null)
            {
                _ui = new PropertiesControl();

                // Apply goes through the router (selection-aware).
                // If current view is the tool model (LineTag), router.Save() handles it.
                _ui.ApplyRequested += delegate { PropertyRouter.ApplyIfPossible(_ui.SelectedModel, _lastCtx); };

                _ps = new PaletteSet(PaletteTitle)
                {
                    DockEnabled = DockSides.Left | DockSides.Right | DockSides.None,
                    MinimumSize = MinSize,
                    Size        = InitialSize,
                    Style       = PaletteSetStyles.ShowCloseButton |
                                  PaletteSetStyles.ShowAutoHideButton |
                                  PaletteSetStyles.Snappable
                };

                _ps.Add("Properties", _ui);
            }

            _ps.Visible = true;

            if (!_hooked)
            {
                var dm = Application.DocumentManager;

                // Attach for current doc (if any)
                if (dm.MdiActiveDocument != null)
                    AttachHandlersTo(dm.MdiActiveDocument);

                // Rewire when document changes
                dm.DocumentActivated += OnDocumentActivated;

                _hooked = true;
            }
        }

        // ---------- Selection & command wiring ----------
        private static void OnDocumentActivated(object sender, DocumentCollectionEventArgs e)
        {
            var dm = Application.DocumentManager;

            // Detach from all open docs (cheap + safe)
            foreach (Document d in dm)
                DetachHandlersFrom(d);

            // Attach to newly active doc
            if (e.Document != null)
                AttachHandlersTo(e.Document);

            RefreshFromSelection();
        }

        private static void AttachHandlersTo(Document d)
        {
            if (d == null) return;

            // Selection events
            d.Editor.SelectionAdded   += OnSelectionAdded;
            d.Editor.SelectionRemoved += OnSelectionRemoved;

            // Command lifecycle (ESC, end, error)
            d.CommandEnded     += OnCommandEnded;
            d.CommandCancelled += OnCommandCancelled;
            d.CommandFailed    += OnCommandFailed;
        }

        private static void DetachHandlersFrom(Document d)
        {
            if (d == null) return;

            // Selection events
            d.Editor.SelectionAdded   -= OnSelectionAdded;
            d.Editor.SelectionRemoved -= OnSelectionRemoved;

            // Command lifecycle
            d.CommandEnded     -= OnCommandEnded;
            d.CommandCancelled -= OnCommandCancelled;
            d.CommandFailed    -= OnCommandFailed;
        }

        private static void OnSelectionAdded  (object s, SelectionAddedEventArgs   e) => RefreshFromSelection();
        private static void OnSelectionRemoved(object s, SelectionRemovedEventArgs e) => RefreshFromSelection();

        private static void OnCommandEnded    (object s, CommandEventArgs e) => ShowToolHome();
        private static void OnCommandCancelled(object s, CommandEventArgs e) => ShowToolHome();
        private static void OnCommandFailed   (object s, CommandEventArgs e) => ShowToolHome();

        // ---------- Core refresh logic ----------
        private static void RefreshFromSelection()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

            var ed = doc.Editor;
            var implied = ed.SelectImplied();

            // Nothing selected → show tool "Home" (LineTag settings)
            if (implied.Status != PromptStatus.OK || implied.Value == null || implied.Value.Count == 0)
            {
                _lastCtx = null;
                BindToolHome();
                return;
            }

            // Use first picked object (expand to multi-select later)
            var id = implied.Value[0].ObjectId;
            _lastCtx = new SelectionContext(id, doc);

            var model = PropertyRouter.Resolve(_lastCtx);
            if (model != null)
                _ui.Bind(model, "Selection");
            else
                BindToolHome(); // unclaimed selection → fall back to tool view
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Clears PICKFIRST and shows the tool "Home" (LineTag settings).
        /// </summary>
        private static void ShowToolHome()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

            try
            {
                // Force-clear implied selection
                doc.Editor.SetImpliedSelection(new Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices.ObjectId[0]);
            }
            catch { /* ignore */ }

            _lastCtx = null;
            BindToolHome();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Bind the palette to the tool settings model so users always see something useful.
        /// </summary>
        private static void BindToolHome()
        {
            // The router already knows how to save this when Apply is pressed.
            _ui.Bind(MasterProperties.LineTag, "Tool");
        }

        // ---------- Size & docking helpers ----------
        public static Size GetSize() => _ps != null ? _ps.Size : InitialSize;

        public static void EnsureFloating()
        {
            if (_ps == null) return;
            if (_ps.Dock != DockSides.None)
            {
                if (_ps.Location.IsEmpty || _ps.Location.X <= 0 || _ps.Location.Y <= 0)
                    _ps.Location = new Point(120, 120);
                _ps.Dock = DockSides.None;
            }
        }

        public static void SetSize(Size size)
        {
            if (_ps == null) return;
            if (_ps.Dock != DockSides.None) EnsureFloating();

            if (size.Width  < MinSize.Width)  size.Width  = MinSize.Width;
            if (size.Height < MinSize.Height) size.Height = MinSize.Height;

            _ps.Size = size;
        }

        // Convenience commands for testing float/dock quickly
        public static void FloatAndResize(Size size)
        {
            Show();
            EnsureFloating();
            SetSize(size);
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        public static void DockLeft()
        {
            Show();
            _ps.Dock = DockSides.Left;
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        public static void DockRight()
        {
            Show();
            _ps.Dock = DockSides.Right;
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_FLOAT")]
        public static void CmdFloat() => FloatAndResize(InitialSize);

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_DOCKLEFT")]
        public static void CmdDockLeft() => DockLeft();

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_DOCKRIGHT")]
        public static void CmdDockRight() => DockRight();
    }
}
```

### What this gives you right now
- After **ESC / command end / no selection**, the palette **binds** to `MasterProperties.LineTag` (“Tool” view) instead of going blank.
- When there **is** a selection the palette still binds the resolved model via `PropertyRouter.Resolve(...)`.
- Your existing **Apply** continues to work:  
  - If bound to a selection, the matching provider runs.  
  - If bound to tool settings (`MasterProperties.LineTag`), `PropertyRouter.ApplyIfPossible` calls `MasterProperties.Save()` (your existing logic).

---

If you want the **“Line next” / “Tag next”** preview labels on the palette too, I can add a tiny non-breaking patch to `PropertiesControl` that only introduces two `ToolStripLabel`s and a `RefreshHomePreview(prefix)` method—just say the word and I’ll supply that as a separate, safe drop-in.

## Response:
10/6/2025, 4:58:05 PM

Absolutely — here’s a **drop-in** `PropertiesControl.cs` that matches your hub style, keeps all your existing behavior (Apply/Revert/Save, presets, resize grip, etc.), and adds a tiny **“Home”** mode with non-incrementing previews:

- New public APIs:
  - `ShowHome(string prefix)`
  - `RefreshHomePreview(string prefix)`
- Two new `ToolStripLabel`s on the right side of the toolbar:
  - `Line next: <peek>`
  - `Tag next:  <peek>`
- When the grid edits **`LineTagSettings.Prefix`**, the preview updates live.

It does **not** change your binding/Apply plumbing.

```csharp
// v0.2.0 (C# 7.3) — PropertyGrid UI with “Home” preview (Line/Tag next)
// - Adds ShowHome(prefix) and RefreshHomePreview(prefix)
// - Two right-aligned ToolStrip labels show non-incrementing peeks
// - Live refresh when LineTagSettings.Prefix changes

using System;
using System.ComponentModel;
using System.IO;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using System.Drawing;                      // Point/Size/Color/Cursors
using Newtonsoft.Json;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;        // NodLineNumberStore

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public partial class PropertiesControl : UserControl
    {
        private readonly PropertyGrid _grid = new PropertyGrid();
        private readonly ToolStrip _bar = new ToolStrip();
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lbl = new ToolStripLabel("Source:");
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblSource = new ToolStripLabel("—");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnApply = new ToolStripButton("Apply");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnRevert = new ToolStripButton("Revert");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnSave = new ToolStripButton("Save");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnLoad = new ToolStripButton("Load");
        private readonly ToolStripSeparator _sep = new ToolStripSeparator();
        private readonly ToolStripControlHost _chkAutoHost;
        private readonly CheckBox _chkAuto = new CheckBox { Text = "Auto-apply", Checked = true };

        // NEW: preview labels (right side)
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblLineNext = new ToolStripLabel();
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblTagNext  = new ToolStripLabel();

        private object _currentModel;
        private object _snapshot;

        // --- resize grip state ---
        private readonly Panel _grip = new Panel();
        private bool _dragging;
        private Point _dragStartScreen;
        private Size _startSize;

        public event EventHandler ApplyRequested;
        public object SelectedModel { get { return _currentModel; } }

        public PropertiesControl()
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill;

            _grid.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
            _grid.PropertyValueChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                // Always refresh previews if prefix changed on tool model
                var name = e.ChangedItem?.PropertyDescriptor?.Name;
                if (string.Equals(name, nameof(LineTagSettings.Prefix), StringComparison.Ordinal))
                {
                    var lt = _currentModel as LineTagSettings;
                    if (lt != null) RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
                }

                if (_chkAuto.Checked && ApplyRequested != null)
                    ApplyRequested(this, EventArgs.Empty);
            };

            _chkAutoHost = new ToolStripControlHost(_chkAuto) { Margin = new Padding(8, 2, 4, 2) };
            _btnApply.Click  += (s, e) => { if (ApplyRequested != null) ApplyRequested(this, EventArgs.Empty); };
            _btnRevert.Click += (s, e) => Rebind(_snapshot);
            _btnSave.Click   += (s, e) => SavePreset();
            _btnLoad.Click   += (s, e) => LoadPreset();

            // Toolbar composition (left to right)
            _bar.Items.Add(_lbl);
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblSource);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnApply);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnRevert);
            _bar.Items.Add(_sep);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnSave);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnLoad);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
            _bar.Items.Add(_chkAutoHost);

            // NEW: previews on the right
            _lblLineNext.Alignment = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right;
            _lblTagNext.Alignment  = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right;
            _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
            _lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag next: —";
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblLineNext);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("  ") { Alignment = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right });
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblTagNext);

            _bar.Dock = DockStyle.Top;

            Controls.Add(_grid);
            Controls.Add(_bar);

            // --- resize grip setup (bottom-right corner) ---
            _grip.Size = new Size(14, 14);
            _grip.Anchor = AnchorStyles.Bottom | AnchorStyles.Right;
            _grip.Cursor = Cursors.SizeNWSE;
            _grip.BackColor = Color.Transparent;
            _grip.Location = new Point(Width - _grip.Width - 2, Height - _grip.Height - 2);

            _grip.MouseDown += (s, e) =>
            {
                if (e.Button != MouseButtons.Left) return;
                CbiPropertiesPalette.EnsureFloating();  // make sure we’re floating
                _dragging = true;
                _dragStartScreen = Cursor.Position;
                _startSize = CbiPropertiesPalette.GetSize();
                _grip.Capture = true;
            };
            _grip.MouseMove += (s, e) =>
            {
                if (!_dragging) return;
                var cur = Cursor.Position;
                int dx = cur.X - _dragStartScreen.X;
                int dy = cur.Y - _dragStartScreen.Y;
                var newSize = new Size(_startSize.Width + dx, _startSize.Height + dy);
                CbiPropertiesPalette.SetSize(newSize);
            };
            _grip.MouseUp += (s, e) =>
            {
                _dragging = false;
                _grip.Capture = false;
            };
            this.Resize += (s, e) =>
            {
                _grip.Location = new Point(Width - _grip.Width - 2, Height - _grip.Height - 2);
            };

            // Second handler (yours) kept: force apply for certain props
            _grid.PropertyValueChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                _grid.Refresh();

                var propName = e.ChangedItem?.PropertyDescriptor?.Name;
                bool forceApply =
                    string.Equals(propName, nameof(PipeRunProperties.LayerName), StringComparison.Ordinal) ||
                    string.Equals(propName, nameof(PipeRunProperties.PipingRunType), StringComparison.Ordinal);

                if (_chkAuto.Checked || forceApply)
                    ApplyRequested?.Invoke(this, EventArgs.Empty);
            };

            Controls.Add(_grip);
        }

        // --------- Public palette-facing API ---------

        /// <summary>Hard clear (rare). Normally use ShowHome(prefix).</summary>
        public void Clear()
        {
            _currentModel = null;
            _snapshot = null;
            _grid.SelectedObject = null;
            _lblSource.Text = "—";
            _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
            _lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag next: —";
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// “Home” view: show tool settings with live previews (non-incrementing).
        /// </summary>
        public void ShowHome(string prefix)
        {
            Bind(new Placeholder(), "Tool");     // keep your placeholder text
            RefreshHomePreview(prefix);
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Updates the non-incrementing number previews (LINE/TAG) using the given prefix.
        /// Safe to call any time; errors are swallowed.
        /// </summary>
        public void RefreshHomePreview(string prefix)
        {
            try
            {
                var p = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(prefix) ? "PR-" : prefix;
                var line = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", p, 4);
                var tag  = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG",  p, 4);
                _lblLineNext.Text = $"Line next: {line}";
                _lblTagNext.Text  = $"Tag next: {tag}";
            }
            catch
            {
                _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
                _lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag next: —";
            }
        }

        public void Bind(object model, string sourceLabel)
        {
            if (model == null) model = new Placeholder();
            _currentModel = model;
            _snapshot = DeepClone(model);
            _grid.SelectedObject = _currentModel;
            _lblSource.Text = string.IsNullOrEmpty(sourceLabel) ? InferLabel(model) : sourceLabel;

            // If we’re binding the tool settings, refresh preview from its prefix
            var lt = model as LineTagSettings;
            if (lt != null) RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
        }

        // --------- Private helpers (unchanged behavior) ---------

        private void Rebind(object snap)
        {
            _currentModel = DeepClone(snap ?? new Placeholder());
            _grid.SelectedObject = _currentModel;

            var lt = _currentModel as LineTagSettings;
            if (lt != null) RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
        }

        private static object DeepClone(object instance)
        {
            if (instance == null) return null;
            var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(instance);
            return JsonConvert.DeserializeObject(json, instance.GetType());
        }

        private string InferLabel(object model)
        {
            return model == null ? "—" : model.GetType().Name;
        }

        private void SavePreset()
        {
            if (_currentModel == null) return;
            using (var sfd = new SaveFileDialog
            {
                Filter = "JSON (*.json)|*.json",
                FileName = _currentModel.GetType().Name + ".json"
            })
            {
                if (sfd.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK) return;
                var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(_currentModel, Formatting.Indented);
                File.WriteAllText(sfd.FileName, json);
            }
        }

        private void LoadPreset()
        {
            if (_currentModel == null) return;
            using (var ofd = new OpenFileDialog { Filter = "JSON (*.json)|*.json" })
            {
                if (ofd.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK) return;
                var json = File.ReadAllText(ofd.FileName);
                var loaded = JsonConvert.DeserializeObject(json, _currentModel.GetType());
                if (loaded != null) Bind(loaded, _lblSource.Text);
            }
        }

        private sealed class Placeholder
        {
            [Category("Info")]
            [DisplayName("Tip")]
            public string Message
            {
                get { return "Select an entity or run a tool to see its properties here."; }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### How this works with the palette host you just adopted
- In `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs`, when there’s **no selection** or a command **ends/cancels**, call:
  ```csharp
  _ui.ShowHome(MasterProperties.LineTag?.Prefix ?? "PR-");
  ```
  (The drop-in I gave earlier already does this via `BindToolHome()`; if you prefer, replace that call with `_ui.ShowHome(...)` to also refresh the preview labels.)

- On **Apply**, after your providers run (or when saving tool settings), call:
  ```csharp
  _ui.RefreshHomePreview(MasterProperties.LineTag?.Prefix ?? "PR-");
  ```

If you’d like me to fold `ShowHome(...)` into your `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs` drop-in explicitly (replacing `BindToolHome()`), say the word and I’ll post that tiny edit too.

> Thought for 17s

You didn’t do anything “wrong”—the errors are because **both files** for the same control now contain the same fields and methods.

WinForms splits a control into **two partial classes**:

- `PropertiesControl.Designer.cs` → should contain **only** the auto-generated stuff: the `components` field and `InitializeComponent()` (and maybe `Dispose`).
- `PropertiesControl.cs` → should contain **your logic**: fields, constructor, event handlers, `Bind`, `Clear`, `ShowHome`, etc.

Right now you’ve got our whole class duplicated in **both** files, so the compiler sees two definitions of `Bind`, `DeepClone`, `_bar`, `_lblLineNext`, etc. → all those **CS0111/CS0121/ambiguity** errors.

---

## Quick fix (2–3 minutes)

### 1) Replace **`PropertiesControl.Designer.cs`** with this minimal stub

> This keeps the designer happy but removes all duplicates.

```csharp
// File: PropertiesControl.Designer.cs
// KEEP THIS FILE TINY. Designer-only partial.
// Do NOT declare your own fields/methods here beyond these.

using System.ComponentModel;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    partial class PropertiesControl
    {
        private IContainer components = null;

        protected override void Dispose(bool disposing)
        {
            if (disposing && (components != null))
                components.Dispose();
            base.Dispose(disposing);
        }

        private void InitializeComponent()
        {
            // Intentionally empty. All UI is built in PropertiesControl.cs.
        }
    }
}
```

### 2) Ensure **`PropertiesControl.cs`** holds ALL your real code

- Keep the version I sent (with the toolbar, labels, `ShowHome`, `RefreshHomePreview`, etc.).
- At the very top of the constructor, make sure you call `InitializeComponent();` once:

```csharp
public PropertiesControl()
{
    InitializeComponent();   // <- keep this
    Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
    ...
}
```

> Do **not** define any of your control fields (`_grid`, `_bar`, `_lblLineNext`, etc.) in the Designer file. They live only in `PropertiesControl.cs`.

### 3) Rebuild

You should see the duplicate/ambiguity errors disappear.  
If any “`Application` is ambiguous” errors show up in other files, add this at the top of those files:

```csharp
using AcApp = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application;
```

…and change `Application.DocumentManager` to `AcApp.DocumentManager`.

---

## Why this works

- The compiler now sees **one** definition of each member (logic in `.cs`), while the designer stub just provides `InitializeComponent` and `Dispose`.  
- It matches the WinForms pattern and avoids future “designer regenerates my code” surprises.

---

If you want, paste the **first ~40 lines of your current `PropertiesControl.Designer.cs`** here and I’ll confirm you replaced the right content.

### 🧠 What’s actually happening

You have **two parallel palette implementations**:

| Folder | Purpose | Current Status |
|--------|----------|----------------|
| `Palette\` | Older experimental version (`CustomPropertiesUserControl`, `PropertiesPalette.cs`) | Commented-out or abandoned code — not in use |
| `PropertiesHub\` | Modern, working version (`CbiPropertiesPalette.cs`, `PropertiesControl.cs`, `PropertyRouter.cs`, etc.) | ✅ The correct, active system |

The old `Palette` folder classes are **conflicting** with the new ones because:
- Both define similar UI logic (`PropertiesPalette`, `PropertiesControl` vs `_ui` field).  
- Both register palettes and events (ESC handling, Apply/Revert).  
- The compiler doesn’t know which `PropertiesControl` or `PropertiesPalette` you mean — hence “ambiguous” and “already defined” errors.

So right now, you have **duplicate namespaces and class names** across two folders.

---

### 🧹 Recommended action

Yes — **remove or exclude** the outdated folder.

#### ✅ Option 1 (preferred)
In **Solution Explorer**, right-click the `Palette` folder →  
**Exclude From Project**.

That way, the files remain on disk (for reference), but Visual Studio won’t compile them.  
→ The compiler will then see only the **PropertiesHub version**, which resolves your namespace conflicts.

#### 🧾 Option 2 (if you’re 100% sure you’ll never need it again)
Right-click → **Delete**.  
Safer: rename first (e.g., `Palette_OLD`) and rebuild.

---

### ⚙️ What happens after you exclude/delete

- The `AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub` namespace becomes the **sole palette owner**.  
- All references to `CbiPropertiesPalette`, `PropertiesControl`, etc., will compile cleanly.  
- Your `PluginEntry.cs` and ribbon buttons will continue to call:

  ```csharp
  AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub.CbiPropertiesPalette.Show();
  ```

  - “components already defined”

namespace AutoCAD2020
{
    public class Commands

{
        [CommandMethod("CBI_TagManager")]

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_PALETTE")]

        public static void ShowCBIPropertiesPalette()

            => AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub.CbiPropertiesPalette.CmdShow();

[CommandMethod("CBI_MATCH_PIPERUN")]
        public static void CBI_MatchPipeRun()
            => PipeRunMatchService.RunInteractive();

        // ---- Project / Support scaffolding ----
        //[CommandMethod("CBI_NewProjectSupport")]
        //public static void CBI_NewProjectSupport()
        //    => AutoCAD2020.Utilities.SupportFileServiceCommands.NewProjectSupport();

        //[CommandMethod("CBI_OpenSupportFolder")]
        //public static void CBI_OpenSupportFolder()
        //    => AutoCAD2020.Utilities.SupportFileServiceCommands.OpenSupportFolder();

        // ---- Tagging ----
        [CommandMethod("CBI_AddTag")]
        public static void CBI_AddTag()
            => AutoCAD2020.Services.TagAddService.CBI_AddTag();

        // ---- Line Tagging ----
        [CommandMethod("CBI_PLACELINETAG", CommandFlags.Modal)]
        public static void CBI_PlaceLineTag()
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null)
            {
                Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.ShowAlertDialog("Open a drawing to use PLACELINETAG.");
                return;
            }

            var ed = doc.Editor;

            // 1) Select a LINE or POLYLINE
            var peo = new PromptEntityOptions("\nSelect pipe (LINE or POLYLINE): ");
            peo.SetRejectMessage("\nOnly Line/Polyline supported.");
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(Line), true);
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(Polyline), true);

            var per = ed.GetEntity(peo);
            if (per.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            // 2) Pick label location
            var ppr = ed.GetPoint("\nPick label location: ");
            if (ppr.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            // 3) Compute tangent rotation at pick
            double rot;
            using (var tr = doc.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var ent = (Entity)tr.GetObject(per.ObjectId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                rot = LineTagService.GetTangentAngleAtPoint(ent, ppr.Value);
                tr.Commit();
            }

            // 4) Ensure tag + place label
            var svc = new LineTagService(new NodLineNumberStore(), new TagRenderOptions());
            string tagText;

            using (doc.LockDocument())
            {
                using (var tr = doc.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
                {
                    var ent = (Entity)tr.GetObject(per.ObjectId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                    tagText = svc.EnsureTag(ent);      // writes XData if missing, returns RAW
                    tr.Commit();
                }

                svc.PlaceLabel(tagText, ppr.Value, rot); // MTEXT at point/rotation
            }

            ed.WriteMessage($"\nPlaced line tag: {tagText}");
        }

        //[CommandMethod("CBI_ReportValveLinks")]
        //public static void CBI_ReportValveLinks()
        //    => Services.LinkReportService.ReportValveLinks();

        [CommandMethod("CBI_ValidateValveIds")]
        public static void CBI_ValidateValveIds()
            => AutoCAD2020.Services.TagValidationService.ValidateValveIds();

        // ---- Maintenance / cleanup ----
        //[CommandMethod("CBI_CleanDrawing")]
        //public static void CBI_CleanDrawing()
        //    => AutoCAD2020.Utilities.DrawingCleaner.CBI_CleanDrawing();

private static PaletteSet _sheetSetPalette;

        [CommandMethod("CBI_SHEETSEDIT")]
        public void OpenSheetSetEditor()
        {
            if (_sheetSetPalette == null)
            {
                _sheetSetPalette = new PaletteSet("Sheet Set Editor")
                {
                    Style = PaletteSetStyles.ShowAutoHideButton |
                            PaletteSetStyles.ShowCloseButton |
                            PaletteSetStyles.Snappable,
                    DockEnabled = DockSides.Left
                };
                _sheetSetPalette.Size = new System.Drawing.Size(800, 600);
                _sheetSetPalette.Add("Editor", new SheetSetEditorPaletteControl());
            }

            _sheetSetPalette.Visible = true;
        }

[CommandMethod("DRAWTRUCKFULL")]
        public void DrawTruckFull()
        {
            Document doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            Database db = doc.Database;

            using (Transaction tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                BlockTable bt = (BlockTable)tr.GetObject(db.BlockTableId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                BlockTableRecord btr = (BlockTableRecord)tr.GetObject(bt[BlockTableRecord.ModelSpace], OpenMode.ForWrite);

                string csvPath = "C:\\CBICAD\\truck_full_outline.csv"; // Update this path if needed
                var lines = LineSegmentLoader.LoadLinesFromCsv(csvPath);
                LineSegmentLoader.InsertLinesToModelSpace(lines, btr, tr);

                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

[CommandMethod("SHOWBLOCKATTRIBPALETTE")]
        public static void ShowBlockAttribPalette()
        {
            if (_paletteSet == null)
            {
                _paletteSet = new PaletteSet("Block Attribute Editor");
                _sheetSetControl = new BlockAttribPropPaletteControl(_paletteSet); // Replace with your class name

                _paletteSet.Add("Attributes", _sheetSetControl);
                _paletteSet.Size = new System.Drawing.Size(300, 500);
                _paletteSet.DockEnabled = DockSides.Left | DockSides.Right;
            }

            _paletteSet.Visible = true;
        }

        [CommandMethod("ExportNODToExcel")]
        public static void ExportNODToExcel()
        {
            Document doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            Database db = doc.Database;
            Editor ed = doc.Editor;

            string desktopPath = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.Desktop);
            string filePath = Path.Combine(desktopPath, "NOD_Export.xlsx");

            using (var workbook = new XLWorkbook())
            {
                var ws = workbook.Worksheets.Add("NOD Contents");
                ws.Cell(1, 1).Value = "Key";
                ws.Cell(1, 2).Value = "TypeCode";
                ws.Cell(1, 3).Value = "Value";

                int row = 2;

                using (Transaction tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
                {
                    DBDictionary nod = tr.GetObject(db.NamedObjectsDictionaryId, OpenMode.ForRead) as DBDictionary;

                    foreach (DBDictionaryEntry entry in nod)
                    {
                        string key = entry.Key;
                        DBObject obj = tr.GetObject(entry.Value, OpenMode.ForRead);

                        if (obj is Xrecord xrec)
                        {
                            ResultBuffer rb = xrec.Data;
                            if (rb != null)
                            {
                                foreach (TypedValue tv in rb)
                                {
                                    ws.Cell(row, 1).Value = key;
                                    ws.Cell(row, 2).Value = tv.TypeCode;
                                    ws.Cell(row, 3).Value = tv.Value?.ToString() ?? "(null)";
                                    row++;
                                }
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                ws.Cell(row, 1).Value = key;
                                ws.Cell(row, 2).Value = "(none)";
                                ws.Cell(row, 3).Value = "(Xrecord has no data)";
                                row++;
                            }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            ws.Cell(row, 1).Value = key;
                            ws.Cell(row, 2).Value = "(not Xrecord)";
                            ws.Cell(row, 3).Value = obj.GetType().Name;
                            row++;
                        }
                    }

                    tr.Commit();
                }

                workbook.SaveAs(filePath);
            }

            ed.WriteMessage($"\nNOD exported to Excel:\n{filePath}");
        }

[CommandMethod("CBI_NewProjectSupport")]
        public static void CBI_NewProjectSupport()
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            var ed = doc.Editor;
            var db = doc.Database;

            var root = Path.GetDirectoryName(doc.Name);
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(root))
            {
                ed.WriteMessage("\nPlease save the drawing first.");
                return;
            }

            var supportDir = Path.Combine(root, "CBI_Support");
            Directory.CreateDirectory(supportDir);

            var storePath = Path.Combine(supportDir, "ProjectTagStore.json");
            var readme = Path.Combine(supportDir, "Readme.txt");
            var changelog = Path.Combine(supportDir, "Changelog.txt");

            // Create JSON if missing (v0.4 skeleton)
            if (!File.Exists(storePath))
            {
                var store = new ProjectTagStore
                {
                    Project = new ProjectTagStore.ProjectMetadata
                    {
                        Name = Path.GetFileNameWithoutExtension(doc.Name),
                        CreatedUtc = DateTime.UtcNow,
                        Engineer = Environment.UserName
                    }
                };
                store.Save(storePath);
            }

            // Readme + Changelog (idempotent)
            if (!File.Exists(readme))
                File.WriteAllText(readme,
    @"CBI Support Folder

- ProjectTagStore.json : Systems, ranges, tags (schema v0.4)
- Changelog.txt        : High-level project log (append-only)

Edit Systems in ProjectTagStore.json before placing tags. Example:

""Systems"": {
  ""ETHANE_RECEIPT"": { ""Prefix"": ""V"", ""Pad"": 4, ""Start"": 1001, ""End"": 1099, ""Next"": 1001 }
}
");

            if (!File.Exists(changelog))
                File.WriteAllText(changelog, "");

            // Save JSON path into DWG NOD
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                AutoCAD2020.NOD_X_Data.ProjectTagPath.SetPath(db, tr, storePath);
                tr.Commit();
            }

            // Log
            AutoCAD2020.Utilities.ChangeLog.Append(supportDir, "PROJECT_INIT",
                $"Seeded ProjectTagStore.json (Version={ProjectTagStore.CurrentVersion})",
                $"Path={storePath}");

            ed.WriteMessage($"\nCreated/verified CBI_Support. JSON: {storePath}");
        }

[CommandMethod("CBI_OpenSupportFolder")]
        public static void CBI_OpenSupportFolder()
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            var ed = doc.Editor;
            var db = doc.Database;

            string storePath;
            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                storePath = AutoCAD2020.NOD_X_Data.ProjectTagPath.GetPath(db, tr);
                tr.Commit();
            }
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(storePath) || !File.Exists(storePath))
            {
                ed.WriteMessage("\nNo tag_store.json set for this drawing. Run CBI_NewProjectSupport first.");
                return;
            }

            var folder = Path.GetDirectoryName(storePath);
            System.Diagnostics.Process.Start(new System.Diagnostics.ProcessStartInfo
            {
                FileName = folder,
                UseShellExecute = true
            });
        }

// ---------- PIPE RUN ----------
        [CommandMethod("CBI_MAKE_PIPERUN")]
        public static void MakePipeRun()
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            var ed = doc.Editor;

            var peo = new PromptEntityOptions("\nSelect polyline to mark as Pipe Run: ");
            peo.SetRejectMessage("\nMust be a Polyline.");
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(Polyline), true);
            var per = ed.GetEntity(peo);
            if (per.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            EnsureRegApp("CBI_PIPE_RUN");

            var data = new XDataMap
            {
                ["SchemaVersion"] = "1.0",
                ["PackageItemTag"] = "PR-TEST-001",
                ["LineTag"] = "PR-TEST-001",
                ["Service"] = "Cooling Water",
                ["FluidCode"] = "CW",
                ["MainPipeSize"] = "4 in",
                ["Schedule"] = "40",
                ["Spec"] = "CW-STD",
                ["FlowDirection"] = "End 1 is upstream",
                ["DesignPressure"] = "150",
                ["DesignTemp"] = "90",
                ["ConstructionStatus"] = "New"
            };

            XDataHelpers.Write(per.ObjectId, "CBI_PIPE_RUN", data);
            ed.WriteMessage("\nAdded CBI_PIPE_RUN XData.");
            CbiPropertiesPalette.CmdShow();
        }

        // ---------- INSTRUMENT / TAG ----------
        [CommandMethod("CBI_MAKE_INSTRUMENT")]
        public static void MakeInstrument()
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            var ed = doc.Editor;

            var peo = new PromptEntityOptions("\nSelect block to mark as Instrument: ");
            peo.SetRejectMessage("\nMust be a BlockReference.");
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(BlockReference), true);
            var per = ed.GetEntity(peo);
            if (per.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            EnsureRegApp("CBI_INSTRUMENT");

            var data = new XDataMap
            {
                ["SchemaVersion"] = "1.0",
                ["InstrTag"] = "TT-101",
                ["LoopTag"] = "Loop-101",
                ["DeviceType"] = "TT",
                ["Location"] = "Field",
                ["SignalType"] = "AI",
                ["RangeLow"] = "0",
                ["RangeHigh"] = "250",
                ["Setpoint"] = "120",
                ["Owner"] = "I&C",
                ["CalibrationDue"] = "2026-01"
            };

            XDataHelpers.Write(per.ObjectId, "CBI_INSTRUMENT", data);
            ed.WriteMessage("\nAdded CBI_INSTRUMENT XData.");
            CbiPropertiesPalette.CmdShow();
        }

        // ---------- PIPING COMPONENT ----------
        [CommandMethod("CBI_MAKE_COMPONENT")]
        public static void MakeComponent()
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            var ed = doc.Editor;

            var peo = new PromptEntityOptions("\nSelect block to mark as Piping Component: ");
            peo.SetRejectMessage("\nMust be a BlockReference.");
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(BlockReference), true);
            var per = ed.GetEntity(peo);
            if (per.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            EnsureRegApp("CBI_COMPONENT");

            var data = new XDataMap
            {
                ["SchemaVersion"] = "1.0",
                ["ComponentTag"] = "V-001",
                ["ComponentType"] = "Valve",
                ["Size"] = "4 in",
                ["Rating"] = "150",
                ["EndConnection"] = "RF",
                ["ValveType"] = "Ball",
                ["Operator"] = "Lever",
                ["FailAction"] = "FC",
                ["ServiceCritical"] = "false"
            };

            XDataHelpers.Write(per.ObjectId, "CBI_COMPONENT", data);
            ed.WriteMessage("\nAdded CBI_COMPONENT XData.");
            CbiPropertiesPalette.CmdShow();
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_LABEL_MAKE")]
        public static void CmdMake() => LabelLinkService.CreateLinkedLabel();

        [CommandMethod("CBI_MAKE_LABEL")]
        public static void CBI_Make_Label()
            => SmartLabelService.CreateSmartLabel();

        // (optional) if you want the refresh-all under one roof:
        [CommandMethod("CBI_LABEL_REFRESHALL")]
        public static void CBI_Label_RefreshAll()
            => LabelLinkService.RefreshAllInCurrentSpace();

        // --- ensure RegApp exists so 1001 name is valid ---
        private static void EnsureRegApp(string appName)
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            var db = doc.Database;

            using (var tr = db.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var rat = (RegAppTable)tr.GetObject(db.RegAppTableId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                if (!rat.Has(appName))
                {
                    rat.UpgradeOpen();
                    var rec = new RegAppTableRecord { Name = appName };
                    rat.Add(rec);
                    tr.AddNewlyCreatedDBObject(rec, true);
                }
                tr.Commit();
            }
        }

    }
}

// File: LineTagCommands.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Commands
// Version: 1.0.0
// Changelog:
//  - 1.0.0: CBI PLACELINETAG: pick line/polyline & point, ensure tag, place label aligned.

using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Geometry;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Rendering;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;
using AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Commands
{
    public class LineTagCommands
    {
        [CommandMethod("CBI", "PLACELINETAG", CommandFlags.Modal)]
        public void PlaceLineTag()
        {
            var doc = Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null)
            {
                Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices.Application.ShowAlertDialog(
                    "No active drawing open. Open a drawing and try again.");
                return;
            }

            var ed = doc.Editor;

            // 1) Pick target line/polyline
            var peo = new PromptEntityOptions("\nSelect pipe (LINE or POLYLINE): ");
            peo.SetRejectMessage("\nOnly Line or Polyline are supported.");
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(Line), true);
            peo.AddAllowedClass(typeof(Polyline), true);

            var per = ed.GetEntity(peo);
            if (per.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            // 2) Pick label point
            var ppr = ed.GetPoint("\nPick label location: ");
            if (ppr.Status != PromptStatus.OK) return;

            // 3) Compute rotation from curve tangent at pick
            double rot = 0.0;
            using (var tr = doc.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
            {
                var ent = (Entity)tr.GetObject(per.ObjectId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                rot = LineTagService.GetTangentAngleAtPoint(ent, ppr.Value);
                tr.Commit();
            }

            // 4) Ensure tag & place label
            var svc = new LineTagService(new NodLineNumberStore(), new TagRenderOptions());
            string tag = string.Empty;

            using (doc.LockDocument())
            {
                using (var tr = doc.TransactionManager.StartTransaction())
                {
                    var ent = (Entity)tr.GetObject(per.ObjectId, OpenMode.ForRead);
                    tag = svc.EnsureTag(ent);
                    tr.Commit();
                }
                svc.PlaceLabel(tag, ppr.Value, rot);
            }

            ed.WriteMessage($"\nPlaced line tag: {tag}");
        }
    }
}

// v0.2.0 (C# 7.3) — PropertyGrid UI with “Home” preview (Line/Tag next)
// - Adds ShowHome(prefix) and RefreshHomePreview(prefix)
// - Two right-aligned ToolStrip labels show non-incrementing peeks
// - Live refresh when LineTagSettings.Prefix changes

using System;
using System.ComponentModel;
using System.IO;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using System.Drawing;                      // Point/Size/Color/Cursors
using Newtonsoft.Json;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;        // NodLineNumberStore

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public partial class PropertiesControl : UserControl
    {
        private readonly PropertyGrid _grid = new PropertyGrid();
        private readonly ToolStrip _bar = new ToolStrip();
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lbl = new ToolStripLabel("Source:");
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblSource = new ToolStripLabel("—");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnApply = new ToolStripButton("Apply");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnRevert = new ToolStripButton("Revert");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnSave = new ToolStripButton("Save");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnLoad = new ToolStripButton("Load");
        private readonly ToolStripSeparator _sep = new ToolStripSeparator();
        private readonly ToolStripControlHost _chkAutoHost;
        private readonly CheckBox _chkAuto = new CheckBox { Text = "Auto-apply", Checked = true };

        // NEW: preview labels (right side)
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblLineNext = new ToolStripLabel();
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblTagNext = new ToolStripLabel();

        private object _currentModel;
        private object _snapshot;

        // --- resize grip state ---
        private readonly Panel _grip = new Panel();
        private bool _dragging;
        private Point _dragStartScreen;
        private Size _startSize;

        public event EventHandler ApplyRequested;
        public object SelectedModel { get { return _currentModel; } }

        public PropertiesControl()
        {
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill;

            _grid.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
            _grid.PropertyValueChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                // Always refresh previews if prefix changed on tool model
                var name = e.ChangedItem?.PropertyDescriptor?.Name;
                if (string.Equals(name, nameof(LineTagSettings.Prefix), StringComparison.Ordinal))
                {
                    var lt = _currentModel as LineTagSettings;
                    if (lt != null) RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
                }

                if (_chkAuto.Checked && ApplyRequested != null)
                    ApplyRequested(this, EventArgs.Empty);
            };

            _chkAutoHost = new ToolStripControlHost(_chkAuto) { Margin = new Padding(8, 2, 4, 2) };
            _btnApply.Click += (s, e) => { if (ApplyRequested != null) ApplyRequested(this, EventArgs.Empty); };
            _btnRevert.Click += (s, e) => Rebind(_snapshot);
            _btnSave.Click += (s, e) => SavePreset();
            _btnLoad.Click += (s, e) => LoadPreset();

            // Toolbar composition (left to right)
            _bar.Items.Add(_lbl);
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblSource);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnApply);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnRevert);
            _bar.Items.Add(_sep);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnSave);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnLoad);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
            _bar.Items.Add(_chkAutoHost);

            // NEW: previews on the right
            _lblLineNext.Alignment = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right;
            _lblTagNext.Alignment = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right;
            _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
            _lblTagNext.Text = "Tag next: —";
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblLineNext);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("  ") { Alignment = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right });
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblTagNext);

            _bar.Dock = DockStyle.Top;

            Controls.Add(_grid);
            Controls.Add(_bar);

            // --- resize grip setup (bottom-right corner) ---
            _grip.Size = new Size(14, 14);
            _grip.Anchor = AnchorStyles.Bottom | AnchorStyles.Right;
            _grip.Cursor = Cursors.SizeNWSE;
            _grip.BackColor = Color.Transparent;
            _grip.Location = new Point(Width - _grip.Width - 2, Height - _grip.Height - 2);

            _grip.MouseDown += (s, e) =>
            {
                if (e.Button != MouseButtons.Left) return;
                CbiPropertiesPalette.EnsureFloating();  // make sure we’re floating
                _dragging = true;
                _dragStartScreen = Cursor.Position;
                _startSize = CbiPropertiesPalette.GetSize();
                _grip.Capture = true;
            };
            _grip.MouseMove += (s, e) =>
            {
                if (!_dragging) return;
                var cur = Cursor.Position;
                int dx = cur.X - _dragStartScreen.X;
                int dy = cur.Y - _dragStartScreen.Y;
                var newSize = new Size(_startSize.Width + dx, _startSize.Height + dy);
                CbiPropertiesPalette.SetSize(newSize);
            };
            _grip.MouseUp += (s, e) =>
            {
                _dragging = false;
                _grip.Capture = false;
            };
            this.Resize += (s, e) =>
            {
                _grip.Location = new Point(Width - _grip.Width - 2, Height - _grip.Height - 2);
            };

            // Second handler (yours) kept: force apply for certain props
            _grid.PropertyValueChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                _grid.Refresh();

                var propName = e.ChangedItem?.PropertyDescriptor?.Name;
                bool forceApply =
                    string.Equals(propName, nameof(PipeRunProperties.LayerName), StringComparison.Ordinal) ||
                    string.Equals(propName, nameof(PipeRunProperties.PipingRunType), StringComparison.Ordinal);

                if (_chkAuto.Checked || forceApply)
                    ApplyRequested?.Invoke(this, EventArgs.Empty);
            };

            Controls.Add(_grip);
        }

        // --------- Public palette-facing API ---------

        /// <summary>Hard clear (rare). Normally use ShowHome(prefix).</summary>
        public void Clear()
        {
            _currentModel = null;
            _snapshot = null;
            _grid.SelectedObject = null;
            _lblSource.Text = "—";
            _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
            _lblTagNext.Text = "Tag next: —";
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// “Home” view: show tool settings with live previews (non-incrementing).
        /// </summary>
        public void ShowHome(string prefix)
        {
            Bind(new Placeholder(), "Tool");     // keep your placeholder text
            RefreshHomePreview(prefix);
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Updates the non-incrementing number previews (LINE/TAG) using the given prefix.
        /// Safe to call any time; errors are swallowed.
        /// </summary>
        public void RefreshHomePreview(string prefix)
        {
            try
            {
                var p = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(prefix) ? "PR-" : prefix;
                var line = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", p, 4);
                var tag = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG", p, 4);
                _lblLineNext.Text = $"Line next: {line}";
                _lblTagNext.Text = $"Tag next: {tag}";
            }
            catch
            {
                _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
                _lblTagNext.Text = "Tag next: —";
            }
        }

        public void Bind(object model, string sourceLabel)
        {
            if (model == null) model = new Placeholder();
            _currentModel = model;
            _snapshot = DeepClone(model);
            _grid.SelectedObject = _currentModel;
            _lblSource.Text = string.IsNullOrEmpty(sourceLabel) ? InferLabel(model) : sourceLabel;

            // If we’re binding the tool settings, refresh preview from its prefix
            var lt = model as LineTagSettings;
            if (lt != null) RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
        }

        // --------- Private helpers (unchanged behavior) ---------

        private void Rebind(object snap)
        {
            _currentModel = DeepClone(snap ?? new Placeholder());
            _grid.SelectedObject = _currentModel;

            var lt = _currentModel as LineTagSettings;
            if (lt != null) RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
        }

        private static object DeepClone(object instance)
        {
            if (instance == null) return null;
            var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(instance);
            return JsonConvert.DeserializeObject(json, instance.GetType());
        }

        private string InferLabel(object model)
        {
            return model == null ? "—" : model.GetType().Name;
        }

        private void SavePreset()
        {
            if (_currentModel == null) return;
            using (var sfd = new SaveFileDialog
            {
                Filter = "JSON (*.json)|*.json",
                FileName = _currentModel.GetType().Name + ".json"
            })
            {
                if (sfd.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK) return;
                var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(_currentModel, Formatting.Indented);
                File.WriteAllText(sfd.FileName, json);
            }
        }

        private void LoadPreset()
        {
            if (_currentModel == null) return;
            using (var ofd = new OpenFileDialog { Filter = "JSON (*.json)|*.json" })
            {
                if (ofd.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK) return;
                var json = File.ReadAllText(ofd.FileName);
                var loaded = JsonConvert.DeserializeObject(json, _currentModel.GetType());
                if (loaded != null) Bind(loaded, _lblSource.Text);
            }
        }

        private sealed class Placeholder
        {
            [Category("Info")]
            [DisplayName("Tip")]
            public string Message
            {
                get { return "Select an entity or run a tool to see its properties here."; }
            }
        }
    }
}

## 1) Make `CbiPropertiesPalette` visible (so `Commands.cs` can call it)

Your errors show:
- `The name 'CbiPropertiesPalette' does not exist in the current context`
- `The type or namespace name 'CbiPropertiesPalette' does not exist in the namespace 'AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub'`

That means the palette **class file isn’t being compiled** or its **namespace/class isn’t public/matching**.

Do this:

- Open **`PropertiesHub/CbiPropertiesPalette.cs`**  
  Confirm the header is exactly:

```csharp
namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public static class CbiPropertiesPalette   // must be public
    {
        // Your palette code...
    }
}
```

- In Solution Explorer, click `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs` → **Properties**:
  - **Build Action**: `Compile`
  - **Custom Tool Namespace**: *(leave blank)*

- In **`Commands.cs`** you already have `using AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub;`.  
  You can also bullet-proof calls with an alias:

```csharp
using PropHub = AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub;

[CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_PALETTE")]
public static void ShowCBIPropertiesPalette()
    => PropHub.CbiPropertiesPalette.CmdShow();
```

If this file was accidentally excluded earlier, include it again (right-click → *Include in Project*).

---

## 2) Fix the `NodLineNumberStore` “inaccessible” error (no more `new`)

You are constructing it:

```csharp
var svc = new LineTagService(new NodLineNumberStore(), new TagRenderOptions());
```

The error `inaccessible due to its protection level` usually happens when another assembly/type with the same name has a **non-public ctor**, and the compiler is binding to that one. Easiest, safe fix: **don’t construct it** — call its static `Next(...)` via a tiny adapter.

Add this **once** anywhere in your project (e.g., `TagNumberingStoreAdapter.cs`):

```csharp
// File: TagNumberingStoreAdapter.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services (same as your other tagging code)
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    internal sealed class NodStoreAdapter : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        public int Next(string scopeKey) => NodLineNumberStore.Next(scopeKey);
    }
}
```

Then change your usages:

```csharp
// Commands.cs and LineTagCommands.cs
var svc = new LineTagService(new NodStoreAdapter(), new TagRenderOptions());
```

This uses the **static** counter (which we know works) and avoids ctor visibility entirely.

(Also make sure there’s only **one** `NodLineNumberStore.cs` in your solution.)

---

## 3) Fix the `SmartLabelService` name

Your error list shows: `The name 'SmartLabelService' does not exist in the current context`.

You’re calling:

```csharp
SmartLabelService.CreateSmartLabel();
```

But earlier code/classes in your project were named **`SmartLabelServices`** (plural). Use the actual name that exists in your project:

```csharp
AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services.SmartLabelServices.CreateSmartLabel();
// or add: using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;
```

If your file is truly `SmartLabelService.cs` (singular), keep singular. The error means the **symbol name** you’re calling doesn’t match the **class** that’s compiled.

---

## Optional (but helpful): keep `PropertiesControl` independent of the palette

In `PropertiesControl.cs` you call:

```csharp
CbiPropertiesPalette.EnsureFloating();
_startSize = CbiPropertiesPalette.GetSize();
CbiPropertiesPalette.SetSize(newSize);
```

Those three calls are fine **if** `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs` is compiled. If you want to decouple completely, you can replace them with no-ops or an injected delegate—but once step #1 is fixed, these will work.

---

## Response:
10/6/2025, 5:33:20 PM

> **Correcting CbiPropertiesPalette.cs**
>
> The user’s code shows an error where `CbiPropertiesPalette` is mistakenly declared as a static class deriving from `UserControl`. Static classes can’t derive from other classes, and this class shouldn’t even be a control. Our fix: update the class as a non-control static manager, remove instance members, and ensure proper event wiring. Also, move `PropertiesControl` back to its dedicated file. We’ll provide a corrected version and concise instructions.
>
> Thought for 9s

You’ve accidentally turned **CbiPropertiesPalette** into a `UserControl` and made it `static` at the same time — that’s why you’re getting “cannot declare instance members in a static class” and why `CmdShow/EnsureFloating/GetSize` are “missing”: that file no longer contains the palette **host** we had.

Here’s a clean, **drop-in replacement** for `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs`.  
It’s **not** a control; it’s the palette **manager** that hosts your existing `PropertiesControl`. It exposes exactly the methods your `Commands.cs` calls (`CmdShow`, `DockLeft`, `DockRight`, `EnsureFloating`, `GetSize`, `SetSize`).

Replace the entire file with this:

```csharp
// v0.2.3 — CBI Properties palette host (manager, not a UserControl)
// Drop-in replacement. Do NOT inherit UserControl here.

using System.Drawing;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Windows;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public static class CbiPropertiesPalette
    {
        private const string PaletteTitle = "CBI Properties";
        private static readonly Size InitialSize = new Size(520, 600);
        private static readonly Size MinSize     = new Size(300, 220);

        private static PaletteSet _ps;
        private static PropertiesControl _ui;
        private static bool _hooked;
        private static SelectionContext _lastCtx;

        // ---------- Public entry point (used by Commands.cs) ----------
        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_PALETTE")]
        public static void CmdShow()
        {
            Show();
            RefreshFromSelection();
        }

        // Create (once) and show the palette
        public static void Show()
        {
            if (_ps == null)
            {
                _ui = new PropertiesControl();

                // Apply goes through router (selection-aware)
                _ui.ApplyRequested += (s, e) => PropertyRouter.ApplyIfPossible(_ui.SelectedModel, _lastCtx);

                _ps = new PaletteSet(PaletteTitle)
                {
                    DockEnabled = DockSides.Left | DockSides.Right | DockSides.None,
                    MinimumSize = MinSize,
                    Size        = InitialSize,
                    Style       = PaletteSetStyles.ShowCloseButton |
                                  PaletteSetStyles.ShowAutoHideButton |
                                  PaletteSetStyles.Snappable
                };

                _ps.Add("Properties", _ui);
            }

            _ps.Visible = true;

            if (!_hooked)
            {
                var dm = Application.DocumentManager;

                if (dm.MdiActiveDocument != null)
                    AttachHandlersTo(dm.MdiActiveDocument);

                dm.DocumentActivated += OnDocumentActivated;
                _hooked = true;
            }
        }

        // ---------- Selection & command wiring ----------
        private static void OnDocumentActivated(object sender, DocumentCollectionEventArgs e)
        {
            var dm = Application.DocumentManager;

            foreach (Document d in dm)
                DetachHandlersFrom(d);

            if (e.Document != null)
                AttachHandlersTo(e.Document);

            RefreshFromSelection();
        }

        private static void AttachHandlersTo(Document d)
        {
            if (d == null) return;

            d.Editor.SelectionAdded   += OnSelectionChanged;
            d.Editor.SelectionRemoved += OnSelectionChanged;

            d.CommandEnded     += (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
            d.CommandCancelled += (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
            d.CommandFailed    += (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
        }

        private static void DetachHandlersFrom(Document d)
        {
            if (d == null) return;

            d.Editor.SelectionAdded   -= OnSelectionChanged;
            d.Editor.SelectionRemoved -= OnSelectionChanged;

            // Command events are safe to unhook even if not hooked
            d.CommandEnded     -= (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
            d.CommandCancelled -= (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
            d.CommandFailed    -= (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
        }

        private static void OnSelectionChanged(object sender, SelectionAddedEventArgs e) => RefreshFromSelection();

        // ---------- Core refresh logic ----------
        private static void RefreshFromSelection()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

            var ed = doc.Editor;
            var implied = ed.SelectImplied();

            if (implied.Status != PromptStatus.OK || implied.Value == null || implied.Value.Count == 0)
            {
                _lastCtx = null;
                BindToolHome();
                return;
            }

            var id = implied.Value[0].ObjectId;
            _lastCtx = new SelectionContext(id, doc);

            var model = PropertyRouter.Resolve(_lastCtx);
            if (model != null)
                _ui.Bind(model, "Selection");
            else
                BindToolHome();
        }

        private static void ShowToolHome()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

            try { doc.Editor.SetImpliedSelection(new Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices.ObjectId[0]); }
            catch { /* ignore */ }

            _lastCtx = null;
            BindToolHome();
        }

        private static void BindToolHome()
        {
            // You can change this to _ui.ShowHome(MasterProperties.LineTag?.Prefix ?? "PR-")
            // if you want the preview labels; binding the model alone keeps behavior identical.
            _ui.Bind(MasterProperties.LineTag, "Tool");
        }

        // ---------- Size & docking helpers (used by PropertiesControl) ----------
        public static Size GetSize() => _ps != null ? _ps.Size : InitialSize;

        public static void EnsureFloating()
        {
            if (_ps == null) return;
            if (_ps.Dock != DockSides.None)
            {
                if (_ps.Location.IsEmpty || _ps.Location.X <= 0 || _ps.Location.Y <= 0)
                    _ps.Location = new Point(120, 120);
                _ps.Dock = DockSides.None;
            }
        }

        public static void SetSize(Size size)
        {
            if (_ps == null) return;
            if (_ps.Dock != DockSides.None) EnsureFloating();

            if (size.Width  < MinSize.Width)  size.Width  = MinSize.Width;
            if (size.Height < MinSize.Height) size.Height = MinSize.Height;

            _ps.Size = size;
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_FLOAT")]
        public static void CmdFloat() => FloatAndResize(InitialSize);

        public static void FloatAndResize(Size size)
        {
            Show();
            EnsureFloating();
            SetSize(size);
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_DOCKLEFT")]
        public static void DockLeft()
        {
            Show();
            _ps.Dock = DockSides.Left;
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_DOCKRIGHT")]
        public static void DockRight()
        {
            Show();
            _ps.Dock = DockSides.Right;
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }
    }
}
```

### Important notes

- **Do not** make `CbiPropertiesPalette` inherit `UserControl`. It’s a static manager that hosts your **`PropertiesControl`** (which *is* a `UserControl`).
- Keep your `PropertiesControl.cs` as the control implementation; it can still call:
  - `CbiPropertiesPalette.EnsureFloating()`
  - `CbiPropertiesPalette.GetSize()`
  - `CbiPropertiesPalette.SetSize(...)`

### After replacing the file
1) Rebuild. The “ApplyRequested cannot declare static” and “CmdShow missing” errors will vanish.
2) If you still get `NodLineNumberStore` constructor visibility errors, switch to the small adapter I suggested earlier (or ensure the ctor is `public`). Quick adapter again:

```csharp
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    internal sealed class NodStoreAdapter : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        public int Next(string scopeKey) => NodLineNumberStore.Next(scopeKey);
    }
}
```

Then:
```csharp
var svc = new LineTagService(new NodStoreAdapter(), new TagRenderOptions());
```

If any errors remain, send me the top 5 (code + file + line) and I’ll zero in.

> For CS0117, the `Dispose` issue might be caused by `PropertiesControl.Designer.cs` not inheriting `UserControl`. We gave the right stub earlier, so I’ll check this further.
>
> **Fixing Designer inheritance and namespace issues**
>
> The issue likely lies in the partial class declaration in `PropertiesControl.Designer.cs`. While we defined `public partial class PropertiesControl : UserControl` in the main `PropertiesControl.cs`, it appears the designer file might not be inheriting properly due to a namespace mismatch or missing base class reference. This explains the `Dispose` method error and the missing definitions for `ApplyRequested` and `Bind`. I’ll check the namespaces and partial class declaration!
>
> **Addressing delegate and overload issues**
>
> There’s an issue with the delegate mismatch for `OnSelectionChanged`. It seems I was reusing the same handler for both the `SelectionAddedEventHandler` and `SelectionRemovedEventHandler`, but they're signatures aren't the same. To fix it, I'll create two separate methods `OnSelectionAdded` and `OnSelectionRemoved`.
> 
> Additionally, there's an error related to an argument mismatch in `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs`. It seems like we might be passing the wrong type to the `Add` method, which expects a `System.Uri`. I'll check that the overload is correct and adjust if needed.
>
> **Fixing control and namespace issues**
>
> The error suggests the compiler is trying to match an overload that expects a `System.Uri`, which may be due to missing references to `System.Windows.Forms`. Since `PropertiesControl` is a `UserControl`, I’ll add the necessary `using System.Windows.Forms` and project reference for `WindowsForms`. 
> 
> The issue with the missing `Bind` method might be due to a namespace mismatch, even though we’ve defined it. # 1) `CbiPropertiesPalette.cs` (palette HOST – not a UserControl)

Key fixes:
- Add `using System.Windows.Forms;` so `PaletteSet.Add(..., Control)` resolves (no Uri overload).
- Separate handlers for `SelectionAdded` and `SelectionRemoved` (signatures differ).
- Call your `PropertiesControl` methods that *do exist* (`Bind(...)` and `ApplyRequested` event).

**Replace the entire file with this:**

```csharp
// File: CbiPropertiesPalette.cs
// v0.2.4 — Palette host (manager). Hosts PropertiesControl; not a UserControl.

using System.Drawing;
using System.Windows.Forms;                           // <- needed for Control-based Add
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.ApplicationServices;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.EditorInput;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Runtime;
using Autodesk.AutoCAD.Windows;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    public static class CbiPropertiesPalette
    {
        private const string PaletteTitle = "CBI Properties";
        private static readonly Size InitialSize = new Size(520, 600);
        private static readonly Size MinSize     = new Size(300, 220);

        private static PaletteSet _ps;
        private static PropertiesControl _ui;
        private static bool _hooked;
        private static SelectionContext _lastCtx;

        // ---------- Public entry point ----------
        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_PALETTE")]
        public static void CmdShow()
        {
            Show();
            RefreshFromSelection();
        }

        public static void Show()
        {
            if (_ps == null)
            {
                _ui = new PropertiesControl();

                // When PropertiesControl asks to Apply, route to the active provider.
                _ui.ApplyRequested += (s, e) => PropertyRouter.ApplyIfPossible(_ui.SelectedModel, _lastCtx);

                _ps = new PaletteSet(PaletteTitle)
                {
                    DockEnabled = DockSides.Left | DockSides.Right | DockSides.None,
                    MinimumSize = MinSize,
                    Size        = InitialSize,
                    Style       = PaletteSetStyles.ShowCloseButton |
                                  PaletteSetStyles.ShowAutoHideButton |
                                  PaletteSetStyles.Snappable
                };

                // IMPORTANT: this overload expects a WinForms Control
                _ps.Add("Properties", (Control)_ui);
            }

            _ps.Visible = true;

            if (!_hooked)
            {
                var dm = Application.DocumentManager;

                if (dm.MdiActiveDocument != null)
                    AttachHandlersTo(dm.MdiActiveDocument);

                dm.DocumentActivated += OnDocumentActivated;

                _hooked = true;
            }
        }

        // ---------- Selection & command wiring ----------
        private static void OnDocumentActivated(object sender, DocumentCollectionEventArgs e)
        {
            var dm = Application.DocumentManager;

            foreach (Document d in dm)
                DetachHandlersFrom(d);

            if (e.Document != null)
                AttachHandlersTo(e.Document);

            RefreshFromSelection();
        }

        private static void AttachHandlersTo(Document d)
        {
            if (d == null) return;

            d.Editor.SelectionAdded   += OnSelectionAdded;
            d.Editor.SelectionRemoved += OnSelectionRemoved;

            d.CommandEnded     += (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
            d.CommandCancelled += (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
            d.CommandFailed    += (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
        }

        private static void DetachHandlersFrom(Document d)
        {
            if (d == null) return;

            d.Editor.SelectionAdded   -= OnSelectionAdded;
            d.Editor.SelectionRemoved -= OnSelectionRemoved;

            d.CommandEnded     -= (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
            d.CommandCancelled -= (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
            d.CommandFailed    -= (s, e) => ShowToolHome();
        }

        private static void OnSelectionAdded(object sender, SelectionAddedEventArgs e)   => RefreshFromSelection();
        private static void OnSelectionRemoved(object sender, SelectionRemovedEventArgs e) => RefreshFromSelection();

        // ---------- Core refresh logic ----------
        private static void RefreshFromSelection()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

            var ed = doc.Editor;
            var implied = ed.SelectImplied();

            if (implied.Status != PromptStatus.OK || implied.Value == null || implied.Value.Count == 0)
            {
                _lastCtx = null;
                BindToolHome();
                return;
            }

            var id = implied.Value[0].ObjectId;
            _lastCtx = new SelectionContext(id, doc);

            var model = PropertyRouter.Resolve(_lastCtx);
            if (model != null)
                _ui.Bind(model, "Selection");
            else
                BindToolHome();
        }

        private static void ShowToolHome()
        {
            var doc = Application.DocumentManager.MdiActiveDocument;
            if (doc == null || _ui == null) return;

            try { doc.Editor.SetImpliedSelection(new Autodesk.AutoCAD.DatabaseServices.ObjectId[0]); }
            catch { /* ignore */ }

            _lastCtx = null;
            BindToolHome();
        }

        private static void BindToolHome()
        {
            // If you want the preview labels, call: _ui.ShowHome(MasterProperties.LineTag?.Prefix ?? "PR-");
            _ui.Bind(MasterProperties.LineTag, "Tool");
        }

        // ---------- Size & docking helpers ----------
        public static Size GetSize() => _ps != null ? _ps.Size : InitialSize;

        public static void EnsureFloating()
        {
            if (_ps == null) return;
            if (_ps.Dock != DockSides.None)
            {
                if (_ps.Location.IsEmpty || _ps.Location.X <= 0 || _ps.Location.Y <= 0)
                    _ps.Location = new Point(120, 120);
                _ps.Dock = DockSides.None;
            }
        }

        public static void SetSize(Size size)
        {
            if (_ps == null) return;
            if (_ps.Dock != DockSides.None) EnsureFloating();

            if (size.Width  < MinSize.Width)  size.Width  = MinSize.Width;
            if (size.Height < MinSize.Height) size.Height = MinSize.Height;

            _ps.Size = size;
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_FLOAT")]
        public static void CmdFloat() => FloatAndResize(InitialSize);

        public static void FloatAndResize(Size size)
        {
            Show();
            EnsureFloating();
            SetSize(size);
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_DOCKLEFT")]
        public static void DockLeft()
        {
            Show();
            _ps.Dock = DockSides.Left;
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }

        [CommandMethod("CBI_PROP_DOCKRIGHT")]
        public static void DockRight()
        {
            Show();
            _ps.Dock = DockSides.Right;
            _ps.Visible = true;
        }
    }
}
```

# 3) `NodLineNumberStore` ctor is “inaccessible” → use a tiny adapter

Instead of `new NodLineNumberStore()`, use an adapter that calls the static `Next(...)`. This avoids the ctor visibility entirely and compiles against either version.

**Add this file:**

```csharp
// File: NodStoreAdapter.cs
// Namespace: AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Abstractions;

namespace AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services
{
    internal sealed class NodStoreAdapter : ITagNumberingStore
    {
        public int Next(string scopeKey) => NodLineNumberStore.Next(scopeKey);
    }
}
```

Now update the two places that construct the service.

### A) `Commands.cs` — replace the constructor call

Find:

```csharp
var svc = new LineTagService(new NodLineNumberStore(), new TagRenderOptions());
```

Replace with:

```csharp
var svc = new LineTagService(new NodStoreAdapter(), new TagRenderOptions());
```

(There are two similar spots in your `Commands.cs` and one in `LineTagCommands.cs` — update each.)

### B) `LineTagCommands.cs` — same change

Find:

```csharp
var svc = new LineTagService(new NodLineNumberStore(), new TagRenderOptions());
```

Replace with:

```csharp
var svc = new LineTagService(new NodStoreAdapter(), new TagRenderOptions());
```
