# 1) `PropertiesControl.cs` — full, working control
> Make sure the file path is `PropertiesHub/PropertiesControl.cs` and its **Build Action = Compile**.

```csharp
// File: PropertiesControl.cs
// v0.2.1 — PropertyGrid UI with “Home” preview (Line/Tag next)

using System;
using System.ComponentModel;
using System.IO;
using System.Windows.Forms;
using System.Drawing;                      // Point/Size/Color/Cursors
using Newtonsoft.Json;
using AutoCAD2020.Tagging.Services;        // NodLineNumberStore

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    // IMPORTANT: partial + inherits UserControl
    public partial class PropertiesControl : UserControl
    {
        private readonly PropertyGrid _grid = new PropertyGrid();
        private readonly ToolStrip _bar = new ToolStrip();
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lbl = new ToolStripLabel("Source:");
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblSource = new ToolStripLabel("—");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnApply = new ToolStripButton("Apply");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnRevert = new ToolStripButton("Revert");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnSave = new ToolStripButton("Save");
        private readonly ToolStripButton _btnLoad = new ToolStripButton("Load");
        private readonly ToolStripSeparator _sep = new ToolStripSeparator();
        private readonly ToolStripControlHost _chkAutoHost;
        private readonly CheckBox _chkAuto = new CheckBox { Text = "Auto-apply", Checked = true };

        // preview labels (right side)
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblLineNext = new ToolStripLabel();
        private readonly ToolStripLabel _lblTagNext  = new ToolStripLabel();

        private object _currentModel;
        private object _snapshot;

        // resize grip state
        private readonly Panel _grip = new Panel();
        private bool _dragging;
        private Point _dragStartScreen;
        private Size _startSize;

        public event EventHandler ApplyRequested;      // <— host subscribes
        public object SelectedModel => _currentModel;  // <— host reads

        public PropertiesControl()
        {
            InitializeComponent();        // <— must exist in Designer partial
            Dock = DockStyle.Fill;

            _grid.Dock = DockStyle.Fill;
            _grid.PropertyValueChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                // Keep previews in sync if Prefix changed on tool model
                var name = e.ChangedItem?.PropertyDescriptor?.Name;
                if (string.Equals(name, nameof(LineTagSettings.Prefix), StringComparison.Ordinal))
                {
                    if (_currentModel is LineTagSettings lt)
                        RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
                }

                if (_chkAuto.Checked)
                    ApplyRequested?.Invoke(this, EventArgs.Empty);
            };

            _chkAutoHost = new ToolStripControlHost(_chkAuto) { Margin = new Padding(8, 2, 4, 2) };
            _btnApply.Click  += (s, e) => ApplyRequested?.Invoke(this, EventArgs.Empty);
            _btnRevert.Click += (s, e) => Rebind(_snapshot);
            _btnSave.Click   += (s, e) => SavePreset();
            _btnLoad.Click   += (s, e) => LoadPreset();

            // Toolbar composition (left → right)
            _bar.Items.Add(_lbl);
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblSource);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnApply);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnRevert);
            _bar.Items.Add(_sep);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnSave);
            _bar.Items.Add(_btnLoad);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("   "));
            _bar.Items.Add(_chkAutoHost);

            // previews on the right
            _lblLineNext.Alignment = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right;
            _lblTagNext.Alignment  = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right;
            _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
            _lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag next: —";
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblLineNext);
            _bar.Items.Add(new ToolStripLabel("  ") { Alignment = ToolStripItemAlignment.Right });
            _bar.Items.Add(_lblTagNext);

            _bar.Dock = DockStyle.Top;

            Controls.Add(_grid);
            Controls.Add(_bar);

            // resize grip (bottom-right)
            _grip.Size = new Size(14, 14);
            _grip.Anchor = AnchorStyles.Bottom | AnchorStyles.Right;
            _grip.Cursor = Cursors.SizeNWSE;
            _grip.BackColor = Color.Transparent;
            _grip.Location = new Point(Width - _grip.Width - 2, Height - _grip.Height - 2);

            _grip.MouseDown += (s, e) =>
            {
                if (e.Button != MouseButtons.Left) return;
                CbiPropertiesPalette.EnsureFloating();
                _dragging = true;
                _dragStartScreen = Cursor.Position;
                _startSize = CbiPropertiesPalette.GetSize();
                _grip.Capture = true;
            };
            _grip.MouseMove += (s, e) =>
            {
                if (!_dragging) return;
                var cur = Cursor.Position;
                int dx = cur.X - _dragStartScreen.X;
                int dy = cur.Y - _dragStartScreen.Y;
                var newSize = new Size(_startSize.Width + dx, _startSize.Height + dy);
                CbiPropertiesPalette.SetSize(newSize);
            };
            _grip.MouseUp += (s, e) =>
            {
                _dragging = false;
                _grip.Capture = false;
            };
            this.Resize += (s, e) =>
            {
                _grip.Location = new Point(Width - _grip.Width - 2, Height - _grip.Height - 2);
            };

            // your force-apply props
            _grid.PropertyValueChanged += (s, e) =>
            {
                _grid.Refresh();

                var propName = e.ChangedItem?.PropertyDescriptor?.Name;
                bool forceApply =
                    string.Equals(propName, nameof(PipeRunProperties.LayerName), StringComparison.Ordinal) ||
                    string.Equals(propName, nameof(PipeRunProperties.PipingRunType), StringComparison.Ordinal);

                if (_chkAuto.Checked || forceApply)
                    ApplyRequested?.Invoke(this, EventArgs.Empty);
            };

            Controls.Add(_grip);
        }

        // --------- Public API used by host ---------

        public void Clear()
        {
            _currentModel = null;
            _snapshot = null;
            _grid.SelectedObject = null;
            _lblSource.Text = "—";
            _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
            _lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag next: —";
        }

        public void ShowHome(string prefix)
        {
            Bind(new Placeholder(), "Tool");
            RefreshHomePreview(prefix);
        }

        public void RefreshHomePreview(string prefix)
        {
            try
            {
                var p = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(prefix) ? "PR-" : prefix;
                var line = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE", p, 4);
                var tag  = NodLineNumberStore.Peek("TAG",  p, 4);
                _lblLineNext.Text = $"Line next: {line}";
                _lblTagNext.Text  = $"Tag next: {tag}";
            }
            catch
            {
                _lblLineNext.Text = "Line next: —";
                _lblTagNext.Text  = "Tag next: —";
            }
        }

        public void Bind(object model, string sourceLabel)
        {
            if (model == null) model = new Placeholder();
            _currentModel = model;
            _snapshot = DeepClone(model);
            _grid.SelectedObject = _currentModel;
            _lblSource.Text = string.IsNullOrEmpty(sourceLabel) ? InferLabel(model) : sourceLabel;

            if (model is LineTagSettings lt) RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
        }

        // --------- helpers ---------

        private void Rebind(object snap)
        {
            _currentModel = DeepClone(snap ?? new Placeholder());
            _grid.SelectedObject = _currentModel;
            if (_currentModel is LineTagSettings lt) RefreshHomePreview(lt.Prefix);
        }

        private static object DeepClone(object instance)
        {
            if (instance == null) return null;
            var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(instance);
            return JsonConvert.DeserializeObject(json, instance.GetType());
        }

        private string InferLabel(object model) => model == null ? "—" : model.GetType().Name;

        private void SavePreset()
        {
            if (_currentModel == null) return;
            using (var sfd = new SaveFileDialog
            {
                Filter = "JSON (*.json)|*.json",
                FileName = _currentModel.GetType().Name + ".json"
            })
            {
                if (sfd.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK) return;
                var json = JsonConvert.SerializeObject(_currentModel, Formatting.Indented);
                File.WriteAllText(sfd.FileName, json);
            }
        }

        private void LoadPreset()
        {
            if (_currentModel == null) return;
            using (var ofd = new OpenFileDialog { Filter = "JSON (*.json)|*.json" })
            {
                if (ofd.ShowDialog(this) != DialogResult.OK) return;
                var json = File.ReadAllText(ofd.FileName);
                var loaded = JsonConvert.DeserializeObject(json, _currentModel.GetType());
                if (loaded != null) Bind(loaded, _lblSource.Text);
            }
        }

        private sealed class Placeholder
        {
            [Category("Info")]
            [DisplayName("Tip")]
            public string Message => "Select an entity or run a tool to see its properties here.";
        }
    }
}
```

# 1) Fix `Dispose(bool)` override error  
**File:** `PropertiesHub/PropertiesControl.Designer.cs`

Your Designer partial is still trying to override `Dispose(bool)` but the compiler isn’t seeing the base signature in this merge (common when WinForms partials get out of sync). Easiest fix: make the Designer stub **not** override anything. The runtime doesn’t need it because our control builds itself in `PropertiesControl.cs`.

**Replace the entire file with this tiny stub:**
```csharp
// File: PropertiesControl.Designer.cs
using System.ComponentModel;

namespace AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub
{
    partial class PropertiesControl
    {
        private IContainer components = null;

        // No override here—keep the stub minimal so the partials merge cleanly.
        private void InitializeComponent()
        {
            // Intentionally empty. All UI is built in PropertiesControl.cs.
        }
    }
}
```

> Make sure **both** partials (`PropertiesControl.cs` and `.Designer.cs`) have:
> - Namespace: `AutoCAD2020.PropertiesHub`
> - Build Action: **Compile**
> - In `PropertiesControl.cs` constructor, keep the `InitializeComponent();` call at the very top.

So just point the other command at the same implementation (or delete it).

```csharp

    => LabelLinkService.CreateLinkedLabel();
```

(Alternatively, if you don’t need two commands, delete the `CBI_Make_Label` method entirely.)

## Prompt:
11/3/2025, 3:31:21 PM

“Show me the current workflow schema or architecture summary for this tool.”

## Response:
11/3/2025, 3:31:22 PM

Here’s the up-to-date workflow/architecture snapshot for the **CBI Properties Palette** stack you just compiled.

# What this tool is
A model-driven palette that:
- auto-detects what you selected in the DWG,
- shows an editable model for that thing,
- applies edits back to the drawing (XData + CAD properties),
- and shows “home” previews for the next Line/Tag numbers.

# Main pieces (who does what)

1) **Palette host – `CbiPropertiesPalette` (static)**
- Owns the `PaletteSet` and a single `PropertiesControl` instance.
- Wires document events:
  - `SelectionAdded/Removed` → refresh palette
  - `CommandEnded/Cancelled/Failed` (ESC etc.) → clear palette
  - `DocumentActivated` → re-attach handlers, refresh
- Core flow:
  - On show → build palette → attach handlers
  - On selection → build `SelectionContext(id, doc)` → `PropertyRouter.Resolve(ctx)` → `_ui.Bind(model,"Selection")`
  - On clear/ESC → `_ui.Clear()`

2) **UI surface – `PropertiesControl` (partial)**
- A `PropertyGrid` toolbar UI (Apply/Revert/Save/Load + Auto-apply).
- Raises `ApplyRequested` when:
  - user clicks **Apply**, or
  - Auto-apply is on and a property changes (some props force apply).
- “Home” view: `ShowHome(prefix)` + `RefreshHomePreview(prefix)` display **non-incrementing** previews using `NodLineNumberStore.Peek("LINE")` and `Peek("TAG")`.

3) **Routing & Providers – `PropertyRouter` + `IPropertySourceProvider`**
- `Resolve(ctx)` asks each provider in order until one **claims** the selection and returns a **model**.
- `ApplyIfPossible(model, ctx)` finds the matching provider and writes changes back.
- Current providers:
  - `PipeRunPropertyProvider` (Polyline/2d/3d)  
    - Reads/writes **`CBI_PIPE_RUN`** XData and can set the target **Layer** (via rules or explicit model value).
  - `InstrumentPropertyProvider`, `ComponentPropertyProvider` (present if in solution).
  - `LineTagSettingsProvider` (tool settings; not selection-based).

4) **Tool settings – `LineTagSettings` + `MasterProperties`**
- JSON-backed (local file) settings model with: `TextHeight`, `Layer`, `Prefix`, `AutoIncrement`.
- Shown in the grid when no selection / tool context; drives the preview labels.

5) **Numbering store – `NodLineNumberStore`**
- Per-scope counters under **NOD/`CBI_LINE_STORE`** as `Xrecord(Int32 DXF 90)`.
- API:
  - `Next(scopeKey)` – returns current and persists +1.
  - `PeekValue(scopeKey)` / `Peek(scopeKey,prefix,width)` – read only.
  - `Reset(scopeKey, startValue)` – set “next”.
- Used by UI previews (LINE/TAG) and by line/label services elsewhere.

# Data models & persistence

- **XData (selection-bound):**
  - `CBI_PIPE_RUN` keys (examples): `LayerName`, `FluidCode`, `FluidSystem`, `PlantGroupName`, `PipingRunType` (enum as string), `NominalDiameter`, `PipingMaterialClass`, `InsulationPurpose`, computed `ItemTag`, etc.
  - Similar patterns for `CBI_INSTRUMENT`, `CBI_COMPONENT` providers.

- **NOD:**
  - `CBI_LINE_STORE` → one `Xrecord(Int32)` per sanitized scope key (e.g., `"LINE"`, `"TAG"`, or project/system scopes).

- **JSON (tool prefs):**
  - `LineTagSettings.json` beside the app/dwg (your Save/Load buttons export/import any model to JSON too).

# Event-driven flow (happy path)

1. User runs `CBI_PROP_PALETTE` → palette shows; handlers attached.  
2. User selects an entity → `Resolve(ctx)` chooses a provider → palette binds its **model**.  
3. User edits values in the grid:  
   - If Auto-apply ON (or property forces apply) → `ApplyRequested`.  
4. `PropertyRouter.ApplyIfPossible(model, ctx)` → provider:
   - writes XData (schema),  
   - applies CAD edits (e.g., layer),  
   - commits.  
5. User presses ESC or finishes a command → palette clears.

# Commands related to this tool (current)
- `CBI_PROP_PALETTE` – show the palette.
- Seeding/testing helpers used during dev:
  - `CBI_MAKE_PIPERUN`, `CBI_MAKE_INSTRUMENT`, `CBI_MAKE_COMPONENT` – stamp XData on picked objects then show palette.

# Extensibility points

- **Add a new provider:** implement `IPropertySourceProvider` (CanProvideFor/GetSelectedObject/Apply), register it in `PropertyRouter._providers`.
- **Add categories/validation:** decorate model properties with `[Category]`, `[Description]`, and add per-property logic in provider `Apply`.
- **More previews:** call `NodLineNumberStore.Peek(...)` for additional scopes (e.g., per-system counters).

# Guardrails & behaviors you asked for (kept)

- Clear palette on ESC and on any command end/fail/cancel.  
- Only first selected object is bound (multi-select can be added later).  
- Minimal Designer stub; all UI is code-built to avoid designer merge issues.  
- Palette size/docking helpers with a manual resize grip.

If you want, I can generate a tiny ASCII sequence diagram or add a “provider checklist” (what to implement, where to register, minimal XData map) to drop into your Obsidian notes.

## 🧩 CBI Properties Palette — Workflow Schema

```text
┌───────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ USER ACTIONS (AutoCAD Environment)        │
│-------------------------------------------│
│  • Run CBI_PROP_PALETTE                    │
│  • Select entity / ESC / switch drawings   │
└───────────────────────────────────────────┘
                  │
                  ▼
┌───────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  CbiPropertiesPalette (static host)       │
│-------------------------------------------│
│  • Creates PaletteSet + PropertiesControl  │
│  • Hooks document + selection events       │
│  • Calls PropertyRouter.Resolve(ctx)       │
│  • Routes ApplyRequested back to Apply()   │
└───────────────────────────────────────────┘
                  │
                  ▼
┌───────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  PropertiesControl (UI)                   │
│-------------------------------------------│
│  • PropertyGrid + Toolbar (Apply/Revert)  │
│  • Shows current model or "Home" preview  │
│  • Emits ApplyRequested on change         │
│  • Supports Save/Load JSON presets        │
│  • Resizable with bottom-right grip       │
└───────────────────────────────────────────┘
                  │
                  ▼
┌───────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  PropertyRouter                           │
│-------------------------------------------│
│  • Keeps a list of IPropertySourceProviders│
│  • Resolve(ctx) → return model             │
│  • ApplyIfPossible(model, ctx) → Provider  │
└───────────────────────────────────────────┘
                  │
                  ▼
┌───────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Providers (per-object type)              │
│-------------------------------------------│
│  • PipeRunPropertyProvider → CBI_PIPE_RUN  │
│  • ComponentPropertyProvider → COMPONENT   │
│  • InstrumentPropertyProvider → INSTRUMENT │
│  • LineTagSettingsProvider → tool settings │
└───────────────────────────────────────────┘
                  │
                  ▼
┌───────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Persistence Layers                       │
│-------------------------------------------│
│  • XData (per-entity)                     │
│  • NOD (NodLineNumberStore counters)      │
│  • JSON (tool settings presets)           │
└───────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

## 🧠 Provider Checklist

| Step | Purpose | Implementation |
|------|----------|----------------|
| **1. Model** | Define the data shape to show in grid | Plain C# class with properties and `[Category]`, `[Description]` attributes |
| **2. Provider class** | Implement `IPropertySourceProvider` | `CanProvideFor()`, `GetSelectedObject()`, `Apply()` |
| **3. Registration** | Register in `PropertyRouter._providers` | Add `new YourProvider()` |
| **4. Read logic** | From XData or entity state | Use `XDataHelpers.Read(ctx.Id, "AppName")` |
| **5. Write logic** | Push to XData or entity props | Use `XDataHelpers.Write(ctx.Id, "AppName", map)` |
| **6. Optional behavior** | CAD edits or post-processing | Example: assign new Layer, update color, rename block |
| **7. Verify UI** | Select entity → palette shows correct fields | Change property → Apply → Confirm DWG updates |

---

## ⚙️ Supporting Subsystems

| Module | Role |
|---------|------|
| **NodLineNumberStore** | Generates and persists numbering counters under `CBI_LINE_STORE` |
| **LineTagSettings** | JSON settings for tag appearance & behavior |
| **TagNumberingService** | Batch auto-numbering using NodLineNumberStore |
| **SmartLabelService** *(future)* | Creates linked label blocks, connects them to entities |
| **MasterProperties** | Singleton for global tool settings (`LineTagSettings.json`) |

---

## 🧱 Key Commands

| Command | Function |
|----------|-----------|
| `CBI_PROP_PALETTE` | Open the CBI Properties palette |
| `CBI_PROP_FLOAT` / `CBI_PROP_DOCKLEFT` / `CBI_PROP_DOCKRIGHT` | Layout test helpers |
| `CBI_LABEL_MAKE` | Create label via SmartLabelService |
| `CBI_LABEL_REFRESHALL` | Refresh all linked labels |
